<div id="page-411">
<h3><a name="page-411">Monday, February  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> some in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on <span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  This evening she <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Come home and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calves</a>.  Brought <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I staid by the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> all the <span class='line-break'> </span> time that I could.  I am <span class='line-break'> </span> hookin a <a href='../subjects/163' title='mat'>mat</a> don't know <span class='line-break'> </span> yet a bout finishin it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is still <a href='../subjects/164' title='improving'>improving</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hope he will soon be well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 45 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-412">
<h3><a name="page-412">Tuesday, February  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> and very <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Some what <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> He went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went with him.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They went on the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and carried some <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a>.  Said he was feeling <span class='line-break'> </span> some better than he had bin.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I do wish that the weather <span class='line-break'> </span> would get good so that I <span class='line-break'> </span> could get out some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie made the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>stove</a> this morning.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a>.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-413">
<h3><a name="page-413">Wednesday, February  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>Clear</a> most of the day and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warmer</a> south <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> blowin.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/165' title='horseshoes'>shod</a> the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/135' title='wood splitting'>split wood</a> some this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I killed a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evenin Josie fixed a <span class='line-break'> </span> box to be solde at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <a href='../subjects/968' title='Straight Stone school'>School House</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> To night Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> went down there.  I hope <span class='line-break'> </span> they may get on OK it is <span class='line-break'> </span> a dark and dreary lookin <span class='line-break'> </span> time to me.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am here with the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They are all a sleep now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-414">
<h3><a name="page-414">Thursday, February  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> hauled <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> and <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> spent the day.  Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I hemed on <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> babys <span class='line-break'> </span> pieces.  I enjoyed my visit <span class='line-break'> </span> so much.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> Bruce and Thelma to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Josie got home <span class='line-break'> </span> from the School House <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning just be fore <span class='line-break'> </span> one oclock.  They said <span class='line-break'> </span> that they had a good <span class='line-break'> </span> time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-415">
<h3><a name="page-415">Friday, February  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evenin.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> hauled <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Cut <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> and sawed wood <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> helped him.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> swept the yard some <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some man passed here today <span class='line-break'> </span> and a greed to take the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> that I bought from <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin.  <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> colte is here tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> today. <span class='line-break'> </span> Have not heard how <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> solde</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-416">
<h3><a name="page-416">Saturday, February  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/176' title='wood sawing'>sawin wood</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> a little.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Made up the bleach that <span class='line-break'> </span> I got from <a href='../subjects/177' title='Charles William'>Charles William</a>s <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/178' title='Charles William&apos;s Store'>Store</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is well enough <span class='line-break'> </span> that he has gone to bed <span class='line-break'> </span> in my room a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-417">
<h3><a name="page-417">Sunday, February 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> nice day.  We all <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Just at night <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a>s to get his team to go <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> after <a href='../subjects/154' title='guano'>guano</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> come to day wants to <span class='line-break'> </span> move to morrow.  He will move <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>house</a> that <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss</a> moved <span class='line-break'> </span> from.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come to see us to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She fixed every <span class='line-break'> </span> thing very nice.  I think all of <span class='line-break'> </span> us enjoyed dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen any of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> folks to day.  Paul sent me <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/125' title='gloves'>gloves</a> to <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mend</a>.  I guess I will <span class='line-break'> </span> mend them tomorrow if nothing happens.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-418">
<h3><a name="page-418">Monday, February 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> with <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a>.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> will stay allnight some <span class='line-break'> </span> where over there.  <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with them.  Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  <a href='../subjects/184' title='Frank Mays'>Frank Mays</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the Island</a> for Ben.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  She finished a <span class='line-break'> </span> bought twelve oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all went up to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A bout all of the snow <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone and it is so <a href='../subjects/186' title='mud'>muddy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> that it is most impossible to <span class='line-break'> </span> travel at all.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-419">
<h3><a name="page-419">Tuesday, February 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> moved <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Sam Owen</a> here today. <span class='line-break'> </span>  <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> brought one <span class='line-break'> </span> load for him.  Ben is up at <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/35' title='cabin'>cabbin</a> now helpin fix <span class='line-break'> </span> up his things.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a>, <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> was with her.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was at school.  They intended <span class='line-break'> </span> to make some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> but <span class='line-break'> </span> could not get what they <span class='line-break'> </span> wanted to fix it with <span class='line-break'> </span> and did not make any.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Some man come today <span class='line-break'> </span> and got the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>Wooding cow</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope he wont be sorry <span class='line-break'> </span> that he got her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-420">
<h3><a name="page-420">Wednesday, February 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> for a load of plunder for <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They got home a bout three <span class='line-break'> </span> oclock in the evening.  He brought <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a>.  Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Laynes</a> this evening to <span class='line-break'> </span> pay some money that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> owed him.  They are fixin <span class='line-break'> </span> to have a <a href='../subjects/193' title='gatherings'>gatherin</a> at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>School House</a> to morrow.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evenin.  They had good luck with <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  I do hope they may do well <span class='line-break'> </span> with their sales.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> bough him a cow to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-421">
<h3><a name="page-421">Thursday, February 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> the time of year.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <a href='../subjects/200' title='Richard Wooding'>Richard Wooding</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shuck corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/38' title='sandwiches'>sandwichs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and her and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>School House</a> and carried <span class='line-break'> </span> them.  They went by <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got the <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> that Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> and Carrie made yesterday <span class='line-break'> </span> and sand witchs that Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> made yesterday.  Josie drove <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was gone two hours.  Did not take <span class='line-break'> </span> the harness off the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> at night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and I and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the School House.  I think they <span class='line-break'> </span> solde a bout all that they <span class='line-break'> </span> had to sell.  There was a <span class='line-break'> </span> small crowd there.  The roads <span class='line-break'> </span> are very bad yet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I could not find my glasses <span class='line-break'> </span> so this is wrote 9 15 <span class='line-break'> </span> Friday morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-422">
<h3><a name="page-422">Friday, February 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day but <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> burnt <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant <span class='line-break'> </span> beds</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He is very feeble.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I do hope he may get <span class='line-break'> </span> better yet.  <a href='../subjects/184' title='Frank Mays'>Frank Mays</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Irvin <span class='line-break'> </span> Lewis</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/244' title='Mrs Mayhew'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/245' title='Laura Mayhew'>Laura Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was at Charles.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To day was the first time <span class='line-break'> </span> that I have bin to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this year.  I hope to go a <span class='line-break'> </span> gain soon.  <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> commenced work at <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Hope he may finish <span class='line-break'> </span> his crop.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 20 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-423">
<h3><a name="page-423">Saturday, February 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning then <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouded <span class='line-break'> </span> up</a> and <a href='../subjects/147' title='hail'>hailed</a> before twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> oclock.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> got up <span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant beds</a> and <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> them.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed a few garments.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> come to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that she came.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She went to see <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evenin.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am always glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> any of them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evenin.  Reese and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> caught <span class='line-break'> </span> the little <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> but could <span class='line-break'> </span> not manage him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-424">
<h3><a name="page-424">Sunday, February 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> this morning.  He keeps <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>mighty feeble</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul<span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> and <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin Reynolds</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> here for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner.  She got a nice <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  Fried <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>ham</a> and <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a>.  She had it all <span class='line-break'> </span> so nice and attractive.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> proud of her fixin so well.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> did not do any thing but keep <span class='line-break'> </span> company.  <a href='../subjects/92' title='Mr Hutcherson'>Mr</a> and <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evenin.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to have them.  Lizzie and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a while and to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> and staid until <span class='line-break'> </span> bed time.  Had a pleasant visit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-425">
<h3><a name="page-425">Monday, February 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> after <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/253' title='fertilizer'>fertilizer</a>.  They got home a bout <span class='line-break'> </span> dark.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> was here to day.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went home this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I washed <span class='line-break'> </span> dishes after dinner.  Josie got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> and washed dishes. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p>  I brought in twenty one <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day the first time since <span class='line-break'> </span> Xmas.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-426">
<h3><a name="page-426">Tuesday, February 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day,  Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went with <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> to <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Henry went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  I have lost the <a href='../subjects/256' title='smoke house'>smoke <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> key.  Ben brought a <a href='../subjects/257' title='key'>key</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> from Blairs but it would not <span class='line-break'> </span> unlock the door.  Don't know <span class='line-break'> </span> what we will do about it yet.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this evening with <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Got their <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> on her <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a snack for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and jobed a round <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day. Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutchersons</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children are <span class='line-break'> </span> all abed and I am going <span class='line-break'> </span> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-427">
<h3><a name="page-427">Wednesday, February 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>Clear</a> by <span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> opened the <a href='../subjects/256' title='smoke house'>smoke <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> door this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> hung up the <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a>.  We have <span class='line-break'> </span> not found the <a href='../subjects/257' title='key'>key</a> yet.  Hope <span class='line-break'> </span> we may find it yet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed some to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and kept the<span class='line-break'> </span> children.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> while.  I was glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> her.  Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to a <a href='../subjects/261' title='cutting match'>cutting match</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening. They cut for <a href='../subjects/262' title='Tom Peak'>Tom <span class='line-break'> </span> Peak</a> at <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Mr Woodings</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-428">
<h3><a name="page-428">Thursday, February 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> until <span class='line-break'> </span> twelve then helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shuck corn</a> all the evenin.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> did a big washin this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> staid with the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie Wooding</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evenin.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin solde his red <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Fifty three years a <span class='line-break'> </span> go to day I was married.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-429">
<h3><a name="page-429">Friday, February 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> day.  It <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a little this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I ironed for while.  She got it <span class='line-break'> </span> and after dinner I finished ironing.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went up to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> this evenin then <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while <span class='line-break'> </span> and to night Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Mr Edmons</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> have not come home yet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid a wake until <span class='line-break'> </span> half after ten.  It is now <span class='line-break'> </span> eleven.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-430">
<h3><a name="page-430">Saturday, February 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> this morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> He is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>very feeble</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> home all day.  <a href='../subjects/340' title='Miss Mayhan'>Miss Mayhan</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here a while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> staid all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They had <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed</a> <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds yesterday.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> gave me a mess of <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They were all well up <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Ben has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  All of our folks has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to bed and I will go soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-431">
<h3><a name="page-431">Sunday, February 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and the children went to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the first time this year.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> went on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  I walked.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> brought me home on the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  <a href='../subjects/269' title='Earnest Craddock'>Earnest</a> and <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/270' title='Willie Moon'>Willie Moon</a> and <a href='../subjects/271' title='George Edwards'>George <span class='line-break'> </span> Edwards</a> was there on a car.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-432">
<h3><a name="page-432">Monday, February 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Josie and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> staid with <a href='../subjects/933' title='Walter Carr'>Mr Carr</a>.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Carr and I went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> on business.  Got back to <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Carrs at two oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and come <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  Got home a bout four <span class='line-break'> </span> oclock.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> come down to see <span class='line-break'> </span> us all.  I would of bin <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to see them and would <span class='line-break'> </span> of bin at home if I had <span class='line-break'> </span> of knowed that they would <span class='line-break'> </span> come.  I was at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to day that poor <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> is worse off want to go and <span class='line-break'> </span> see him soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-433">
<h3><a name="page-433">Tuesday, February 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  Had a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <a href='../subjects/82' title='storm'>storm</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> be fore day.  <a href='../subjects/937' title='Rufus Boscombe Carr'>Mr. Bascome Carr</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> last night.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went down there started abough <span class='line-break'> </span> midnight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I staid here all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben come home this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> done the <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feeding</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and got a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/276' title='rooster'>rooster</a>.  Said <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>his mother</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come home from <a href='../subjects/971' title='Java, Virginia'>Java</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 40 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-434">
<h3><a name="page-434">Wednesday, February 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked until noon <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/937' title='Rufus Boscombe Carr'>Mr Carrs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was down there.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then went with Ben to the <span class='line-break'> </span> burial.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> staid at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  We heard to day that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/280' title='Buck Farmer'>Buck Farmer</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>set</a> three <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening the first that <span class='line-break'> </span> I have set.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day the first <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> that <span class='line-break'> </span> has bin done here this year.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salet</a> for dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> the first that we have had <span class='line-break'> </span> this year.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-435">
<h3><a name="page-435">Thursday, February 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> <a href='../subjects/285' title='corn house'>corn house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.  I wrote <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/302' title='Irvin Craddock'>Irvin Craddock</a> a bout the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a>.  Denia and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> look at the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> and <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> looked at his cows and little <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  It is a beauty.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to night that <a href='../subjects/286' title='Mrs. Oley Hubbard'>Mrs Oley <span class='line-break'> </span> Hubbard</a> is <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>.  Died sudden.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-436">
<h3><a name="page-436">Friday, March  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A nice morning. <a href='../subjects/287' title='windy'>Wind</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> a little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> in the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went to <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a> to help <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shuck corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They finished getting up his corn <span class='line-break'> </span> and finished covering his <a href='../subjects/285' title='corn house'>corn <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> the most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> us.  Josie helped to carry Hazel <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladis Brumfield</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> from <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Josie and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben will come home if nothin <span class='line-break'> </span> happens to him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children are all a sleep <span class='line-break'> </span> now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-437">
<h3><a name="page-437">Saturday, March  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> hauled <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>stalks</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning then Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> and worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/285' title='corn house'>corn house</a> until twelve.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Come home for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening he <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/289' title='colt'>colt</a> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> then <span class='line-break'> </span> got the <a href='../subjects/291' title='locust stump'>locus stump</a> up that <span class='line-break'> </span> was in the yard.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I burnt some <span class='line-break'> </span> brush that was in the garden.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/286' title='Mrs. Oley Hubbard'>Mrs Hubbard</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  None of us did <span class='line-break'> </span> not go to the <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-438">
<h3><a name="page-438">Sunday, March  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried me <span class='line-break'> </span> part of the way to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a>.  I had a good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They had no company.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/305' title='Lillian Peak'>Miss Lillian Peak</a> come be fore I <span class='line-break'> </span> come home.  I started walkin <span class='line-break'> </span> met with <a href='../subjects/951' title='Oscar Brumfield'>Oscar Brumfield</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a> got his <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> and <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and brought me nearly home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> come home <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid at <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> was with me.  Him and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> played all the <span class='line-break'> </span> time we were at Lees.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-439">
<h3><a name="page-439">Monday, March  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Raining</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went and helped to cut<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  I got out <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> that the Blair <span class='line-break'> </span> girls gathered last <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fall</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> they are very nice.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> spent the evening at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Aunt Carries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  Both the children <span class='line-break'> </span> have bad <a href='../subjects/297' title='colds'>colds</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All gone to bed but me.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I soon will be if nothing <span class='line-break'> </span> happens.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-440">
<h3><a name="page-440">Tuesday, March  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shuckin</a> and <a href='../subjects/299' title='corn cribbing'>cribbing</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evenin.  Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to try to sell <a href='../subjects/184' title='Frank Mays'>Frank Mays</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a>.  Mays shucked corn in <span class='line-break'> </span> his place.  Ben brough <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and the baby home from <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrs</a>.  I heard that <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel <span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham</a> has <a href='../subjects/7538' title='Ethel Mae (Polly) Worsham'>a girl born this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night <a href='../subjects/301' title='Frank Blair'>Frank</a> and <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/302' title='Irvin Craddock'>Irvin Craddock</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/303' title='Jim Craddock'>Jim Craddock</a> come here and <span class='line-break'> </span> staid until bed time.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Irvin staid all night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a while <span class='line-break'> </span> this evenin.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to Carries.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-441">
<h3><a name="page-441">Wednesday, March  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  A <a href='../subjects/314' title='thunder cloud'>thunder <span class='line-break'> </span> cloud</a> to night and a little <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley <span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/302' title='Irvin Craddock'>Irvin Craddock</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> bought a <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> here this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  We passed them twice <span class='line-break'> </span> to day on their way home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She made her a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We saw <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:50 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-442">

<div class="page-content">

<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.  I eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home and fixed for <span class='line-break'> </span> company to night.  <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/39' title='Helen Brumfield'>Hellen Brumfield</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/305' title='Lillian Peak'>Lillian Peak</a> come here <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> come they <span class='line-break'> </span> are <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>playing cards</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night there is a <span class='line-break'> </span> light in the north.  I wrote <span class='line-break'> </span> on the wrong page a few <span class='line-break'> </span> nights ago.  <a href='../subjects/316' title='Mrs Kellie'>Mrs Kellie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was at <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  She said <span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/367' title='Odie Kellie'>Otie Kellie</a> was gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> get him a new <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> is in <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/318' title='parlor'>parlor</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 o:clock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-443">
<h3><a name="page-443">Friday, March  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/135' title='wood splitting'>split wood</a> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I staid <span class='line-break'> </span> with the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evenin I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George<span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a>.  They were <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shuckin<span class='line-break'> </span> corn</a> there.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> the children come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>haulin wood</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/320' title='Marvin&apos;s colt'>Marvins colte</a> got in the <a href='../subjects/321' title='pasture'>pasture</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with our <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> but did not get hurt.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

</div>

<div id="page-444">
<h3><a name="page-444">Saturday, March  9, 1918</a></h3>

<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> hauled and <span class='line-break'> </span> cut <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  To night <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait<span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and moved <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/323' title='dog house'>dog house</a> and cleaned <span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/324' title='yard'>yard</a> and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some.  I washed a little.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and two <span class='line-break'> </span> of the Owen children <span class='line-break'> </span> played all evening had <span class='line-break'> </span> a good time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

</div>

<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to meet <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> brother and <span class='line-break'> </span> brother in law.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and spent the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley <span class='line-break'> </span> Hutchersons</a> and eat dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/326' title='Fred Hutcherson'>Fred</a> and <a href='../subjects/327' title='Irvin Hutcherson'>Irvin Hutcherson</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry played with a <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> nearly all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
