<div id="page-446">
<h3><a name="page-446">Monday, March 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cut <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/135' title='wood splitting'>split <span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We drove <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> with us.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come to Carries <span class='line-break'> </span> and would have come here <span class='line-break'> </span> if we had bin at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am sorry that I did <span class='line-break'> </span> not see her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-447">
<h3><a name="page-447">Tuesday, March 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant beds</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> until it rained.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> commenced washing <span class='line-break'> </span> but quit before she finished <span class='line-break'> </span> as the weather was so bad.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie commenced making <a href='../subjects/328' title='bats'>bats</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for her <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  To night <span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> my <a href='../subjects/125' title='gloves'>gloves</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> has a very bad <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-448">
<h3><a name="page-448">Wednesday, March 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> some of the neighbors worked <span class='line-break'> </span> the road that the <a href='../subjects/329' title='mail carrier'>mail carrier</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> travels.  To night Ben has <span class='line-break'> </span> gone to stay at <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a>.  He [is] very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  To night she is <span class='line-break'> </span> sick.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  All four of the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>school teachers</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> spend the night at <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Willie Mayhews</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin Smiths <a href='../subjects/330' title='plum tree'>plum tree</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> is white with bloom.  I am <span class='line-break'> </span> a fraid that the fruit will <span class='line-break'> </span> get killed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:45 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-449">
<h3><a name="page-449">Thursday, March 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy all day.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> there was a <a href='../subjects/82' title='storm'>storm</a>.  <a href='../subjects/331' title='lightning'>Lightning</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> and <a href='../subjects/147' title='hail'>hail</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> helped <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>rais <span class='line-break'> </span> a stable</a> at <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Mr Woodings</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come here this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  She brough some <a href='../subjects/56' title='yarn'>yarn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for me to <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a> <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>socks</a> for the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/334' title='soldiers'>soldiers</a>.  I have commenced <span class='line-break'> </span> to knit.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> have not bin well <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  She made <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come with her home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-450">
<h3><a name="page-450">Friday, March 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7644' title='clearing land'>cleared</a><span class='line-break'> </span> off place for a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> that<span class='line-break'> </span> they <a href='../subjects/7645' title='barn construction'>want to build</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> year.  I went to <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I stayed<span class='line-break'> </span> nearly all day.  Walked home.<span class='line-break'> </span> I come by <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollies</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> had<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> and had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a><span class='line-break'> </span> ready when I got home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was glad I had<span class='line-break'> </span> nothing to do -- I was tired.<span class='line-break'> </span> I finished my first <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>sock</a><span class='line-break'> </span> that I <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a> for the <a href='../subjects/334' title='soldiers'>soldiers</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and commenced another<span class='line-break'> </span> one.  Will be glad when I<span class='line-break'> </span> am done them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-451">
<h3><a name="page-451">Saturday, March 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried me <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> this morning.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> staid with <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> nearly <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  He is very bad off <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag</a> had quite crow[d] to<span class='line-break'> </span> day for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice <span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding</a> <a href='../subjects/337' title='Duckey Kellie'>Mrs Duckey Kellie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/338' title='Sally Strance'>Mrs Sallie Strance</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A <a href='../subjects/339' title='mink'>mink</a> caugh one of my <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> that was setting. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> killed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/340' title='Miss Mayhan'>Miss Mayhan</a> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come here a while.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-452">
<h3><a name="page-452">Sunday, March 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He is very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  There was <span class='line-break'> </span> a lot of callers at <span class='line-break'> </span> Charles.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> Brumfield <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Charles did <span class='line-break'> </span> not come home said he <span class='line-break'> </span> did not have time.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Lee staid with Charles Sunday <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  He had a bad <span class='line-break'> </span> night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-453">
<h3><a name="page-453">Monday, March 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I am still <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a>.  He is very sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/184' title='Frank Mays'>Frank Mays</a> started <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> with the last of Charles <span class='line-break'> </span> crop of <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to Charles s.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Kate had bin down to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smiths</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-454">
<h3><a name="page-454">Tuesday, March 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/341' title='Mr Spruce'>Mr Spruce</a> come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here last night got here <span class='line-break'> </span> after dark.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> fixed <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> for them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was not at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> come to <span class='line-break'> </span> see Charles this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I come with Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  He has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a>.  Josie went with <span class='line-break'> </span> him left the children.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>set</a> three <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-455">
<h3><a name="page-455">Wednesday, March 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  At twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> oclock Josie and Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come by here to day on his <span class='line-break'> </span> way from the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Said that he thought that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> was wors that he <span class='line-break'> </span> was yesterday.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I want to know so bad <span class='line-break'> </span> whoo is with him tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> come down a little while <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> to day <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> did two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>

</div>

<div id="page-457">
<h3><a name="page-457">Friday, March 22, 1918</a></h3>

<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carrs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She gave them several <span class='line-break'> </span> things.  He bought 100 [pounds] of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> for <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-458">
<h3><a name="page-458">Saturday, March 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this morning at <span class='line-break'> </span> half past seven oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I come with <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> home <span class='line-break'> </span> from there.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come here this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>

<div id="page-459">
<h3><a name="page-459">Sunday, March 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the evening.  <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> He was buried in a quiet <span class='line-break'> </span> decent manner in my judge<span class='line-break'> </span> ment.  <a href='../subjects/346' title='Reverend Padget'>Rev Padget</a> talked <span class='line-break'> </span> some at the grave.  There <span class='line-break'> </span> was a large crowd of kinds <span class='line-break'> </span> folks and friends present.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All went home this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> except <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He staid with <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They could not go to sleep <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight for laughing and <span class='line-break'> </span> playing.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-460">
<h3><a name="page-460">Monday, March 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> day the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> blowed most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> hauled <span class='line-break'> </span> rock and laid the foundation <span class='line-break'> </span> of a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> put in a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning we quilted <span class='line-break'> </span> on it some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I commenced an other <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>sock</a> to night that will <span class='line-break'> </span> be 5 pair.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-461">
<h3><a name="page-461">Tuesday, March 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> work on his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut<span class='line-break'> </span> wood</a> for Ben.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and staid <span class='line-break'> </span> with the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>ed <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> was at home by her<span class='line-break'> </span> self.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordia</a> had gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Wren Worshams</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a> was at <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Nettie Blair and <a href='../subjects/41' title='Beulah Brumfield'>Bulah<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all went to <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhews</a> this evening from <span class='line-break'> </span> school.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-462">
<h3><a name="page-462">Wednesday, March 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>Davis s <span class='line-break'> </span> saw mill</a> this morning for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.  <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>Plowed</a> some this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening for a <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe</a> patch.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> finished <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilting</a> her <span class='line-break'> </span> quilt this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a> this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> and come by <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and stoped a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to day that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/350' title='pneumonia'>pneumony</a>.  Hope she may <span class='line-break'> </span> soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-463">
<h3><a name="page-463">Thursday, March 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening he went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/351' title='Mr Worsham'>Mr Worshams</a> with <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/352' title='Jim Doss'>Jim Doss s</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/353' title='Mary Doss'>Mrs Doss</a> was getting on fine <span class='line-break'> </span> so far as I could see.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I come back by <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss</a><span class='line-break'> </span> they were all well. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  I am <span class='line-break'> </span> sorry that I was not at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-464">
<h3><a name="page-464">Friday, March 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A <a href='../subjects/339' title='mink'>mink</a> killed a hen <span class='line-break'> </span> here this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> called the <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Edmons boys</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and they killed the mink.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I have had four <a href='../subjects/282' title='hens'>hens</a> killed <span class='line-break'> </span> lately and lost two <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>settins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> fixed up her <a href='../subjects/354' title='furniture'>furniture</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I worked a little <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> and went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  Ben built a <span class='line-break'> </span> shelter for the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-465">
<h3><a name="page-465">Saturday, March 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and some <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I stoped at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>creek</a> and <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  Did not <span class='line-break'> </span> get but three fish.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Car</a> left her home <span class='line-break'> </span> to day to live a mong <span class='line-break'> </span> her children.  She gave <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie several things.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I bought her <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> paid <span class='line-break'> </span> $50 for her.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> is here to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I think he is ordering some <span class='line-break'> </span> things for his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-466">
<h3><a name="page-466">Sunday, March 31, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim<span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson<span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a>.  They brough me <span class='line-break'> </span> home on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7795' title='Dr Wigginton'>Dr Wiggonton</a> and <a href='../subjects/360' title='Pearl Harvey'>Pearl</a><span class='line-break'> </span> come to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a>.  She<span class='line-break'> </span> was not at home.  She was<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  They went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> A lot of the grand<span class='line-break'> </span> children went on the<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/361' title='mountain'>mountain</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/340' title='Miss Mayhan'>Miss<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhan</a> went with them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-467">
<h3><a name="page-467">Monday, April  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> to day not enough <span class='line-break'> </span> to stop work.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> cover his <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/362' title='easter eggs'>colored</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> for the children <span class='line-break'> </span> and made some <a href='../subjects/328' title='bats'>bats</a> for her <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> was here a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  The children <span class='line-break'> </span> had a time hunting eggs.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I sowed a few <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Eleven oclock by the new time.</p>
</div>

<div id="page-468">

<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washing <span class='line-break'> </span> and finished by twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The three boys and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  I had <span class='line-break'> </span> no business.  He kindly offered <span class='line-break'> </span> to take me.  I had a <span class='line-break'> </span> pleasant evening.  We saw <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/365' title='Mr Rice'>Mr Rice</a> and <a href='../subjects/366' title='Mr Rorer'>Mr Rorer</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>

<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. I come by <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Reynolds</a> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>red hogs</a> <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> came <span class='line-break'> </span> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-471">

<div id="page-472">
<h3><a name="page-472">Saturday, April  6, 1918</a></h3>

<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We did not catch anything.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/373' title='Dr'>Dr</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> this evening.  He <span class='line-break'> </span> thinks that she has <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/374' title='scarlet fever'>scarlet fever</a> in a <span class='line-break'> </span> milde form.  I hope she may <span class='line-break'> </span> soon be well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-473">
<h3><a name="page-473">Sunday, April  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> home to day.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> here with them.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a> all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went with <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nannie Kate</a> to see <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thompson</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I think they are so well <span class='line-break'> </span> fixed for new beginners.  <span class='line-break'> </span> That has bin a grand <span class='line-break'> </span> old place and is good yet.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel Smith</a> is broke out <span class='line-break'> </span> with something the <a href='../subjects/373' title='Dr'>Dr</a> says <span class='line-break'> </span> he thinks it is <a href='../subjects/374' title='scarlet fever'>scarlet <span class='line-break'> </span> fever</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is not well <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Hope they both <span class='line-break'> </span> will be well soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-474">
<h3><a name="page-474">Monday, April  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day and still <span class='line-break'> </span> raining.  The men folks could <span class='line-break'> </span> not do much of any thing. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I put in a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> helped us quilt.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> He is not well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel Smith</a> is better of <span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/374' title='scarlet fever'>breakin out</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Hope they will soon be <span class='line-break'> </span> well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-475">
<h3><a name="page-475">Tuesday, April  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rained</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all day and still raining.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We finished <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilting</a> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> quilt.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> did not go to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> There was to be a <a href='../subjects/388' title='movie'>moving <span class='line-break'> </span> picture show</a> at the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> to night but it is so <span class='line-break'> </span> bad I guess there will not be <span class='line-break'> </span> any one to see it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-476">
<h3><a name="page-476">Wednesday, April 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Men folks could not <span class='line-break'> </span> do any thing out of <span class='line-break'> </span> doors.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Carr</a> <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then knit.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-477">
<h3><a name="page-477">Thursday, April 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very bad day.  It has <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snowed</a> all the evening the <span class='line-break'> </span> ground is white.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men could not do <span class='line-break'> </span> anything much.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished a pair of <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>socks</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for the <a href='../subjects/389' title='Red Cross'>Red Cross</a> ladies.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I have knit ten pair <span class='line-break'> </span> that is all the <a href='../subjects/56' title='yarn'>yarn</a> that <span class='line-break'> </span> I have got.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-478">
<h3><a name="page-478">Friday, April 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>The land was covered <span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/2' title='snow'>snow</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> To night it is all <span class='line-break'> </span> gone.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut some wood</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and ask <span class='line-break'> </span> hands to help <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>rais a barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I hemmed three <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilts</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and beat up the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-479">
<h3><a name="page-479">Saturday, April 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> had a <a href='../subjects/332' title='barn raising'>barn raisin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> had plenty help and got <span class='line-break'> </span> done before night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come and made <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a> and helped <span class='line-break'> </span> wash dishes and that was a <span class='line-break'> </span> job.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> is here <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> hurt her toe <span class='line-break'> </span> right bad to night bringin <span class='line-break'> </span> in some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> and dropped <span class='line-break'> </span> a piece on her toe.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Oh I am so glad the <span class='line-break'> </span> barn is raised.  I thank <span class='line-break'> </span> all that helped.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock by <span class='line-break'> </span> the new time</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-480">
<h3><a name="page-480">Sunday, April 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> staid at home all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They were all well but <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a>.  She had a bad <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a> and did not go to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a> and <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come with them home from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <a href='../subjects/394' title='Claud Hendrix'>Claud Hendrix</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/395' title='Nathaniel Marshal'>Nathaniel Marshal</a> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to Sunday School.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> was not well enough <span class='line-break'> </span> to go.  I come home early <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> my <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We eat <a href='../subjects/396' title='colde supper'>colde supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Carr is here yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben <a href='../subjects/953' title='hair cutting'>cut</a> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henrys</a> hair tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-481">
<h3><a name="page-481">Monday, April 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> brough the things that <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> gave them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Bought roofing for the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> Got home about 2 oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washin.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/398' title='Earnest Lovelace'>Earnest Lovelace</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to Carries this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> to work.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Carr has a <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-482">
<h3><a name="page-482">Tuesday, April 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and a little <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hauled <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a little while.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Reynolds</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> there a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben and Josie and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to see a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/388' title='movie'>moving picture show</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> went with them <span class='line-break'> </span> and will go home I guess.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am uneasy a bout them <span class='line-break'> </span> a fraid the <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> is so <span class='line-break'> </span> rough that they will get <span class='line-break'> </span> stalled.  <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is sick <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  I certainly do hope <span class='line-break'> </span> that he may soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-483">

<p> <a href='../subjects/399' title='Mrs Bailiss'>Mrs Bailiss</a> and <a href='../subjects/400' title='Melvin'>Melvin</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> while we were at dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a> and <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to see their sister <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/402' title='Mrs Short'>Mrs Short</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> called here <span class='line-break'> </span> to night and ask Ben to <span class='line-break'> </span> haul him a load of <a href='../subjects/403' title='brick'>brick</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I think he will haul it but <span class='line-break'> </span> he don't like to a bit.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is better to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-484">
<h3><a name="page-484">Thursday, April 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this morning but none <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> hauled a <span class='line-break'> </span> load of <a href='../subjects/403' title='brick'>brick</a> for <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is still sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night while we were <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> a <a href='../subjects/404' title='wasp'>wasp</a> stung <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>.  She thought it most <span class='line-break'> </span> ruined her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

<div id="page-485">

<div class="page-content">

I <span class='line-break'> </span> dressed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>hen</a> for <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>. <h3><a name="page-489">Tuesday, April 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/135' title='wood splitting'>split</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> up the olde <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> logs <span class='line-break'> </span> and moved the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and picked <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blair</a> come over here <span class='line-break'> </span> for some <a href='../subjects/415' title='vinegar'>vinegar</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice Owen</a> come for <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> for <a href='../subjects/401' title='Virginia Dews'>Mrs Dews</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

</div>
