<div id="page-490">
<h3><a name="page-490">Wednesday, April 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hauled in some <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a>.  Owen <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.  Josie went to <span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/434' title='Mrs Powers'>Mrs Powers</a>.  Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>creek</a> and <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Caught a few fish.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben got stalled and had <span class='line-break'> </span> to have help to get a way.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I picked <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  <a href='../subjects/435' title='James Farthing'>Mr Farthings</a> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come here to day.  Ben put <span class='line-break'> </span> them up.  They got them this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> worked on his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-491">
<h3><a name="page-491">Thursday, April 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William</a> hauled rock to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  I picked <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come in the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I walked with them <span class='line-break'> </span> as far as <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This is wrote the 26 at <span class='line-break'> </span> eight oclock.  I could not <span class='line-break'> </span> find my <a href='../subjects/436' title='ink'>ink</a> last night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-492">
<h3><a name="page-492">Friday, April 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> commenced <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a> a bout <span class='line-break'> </span> 9 in the morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> had commenced to plow but had <span class='line-break'> </span> quit.  <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> come at <span class='line-break'> </span> twelve for Ben to <a href='../subjects/953' title='hair cutting'>cut</a> his <span class='line-break'> </span> hair the[n] he helped Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/437' title='chinking'>chink</a> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> until they got <span class='line-break'> </span> done.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then we both picked <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and finished them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-493">
<h3><a name="page-493">Saturday, April 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  One of the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was sick.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfield</a> all helped <span class='line-break'> </span> him a bout her.  Posie Reynolds <span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> here for the first <span class='line-break'> </span> time in a long time.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/7864' title='Rena Mayhew'>Rena</a> and <a href='../subjects/439' title='Audry Mayhew'>Audry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/440' title='Fessy(?) Mayhew'>Fessy(?) Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia<span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma Owen</a> all come <span class='line-break'> </span> all for <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a> to <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>set</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I did not have but one setting.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia got them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben and Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-494">
<h3><a name="page-494">Sunday, April 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>Cloudy</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> today<span class='line-break'> </span> to an <a href='../subjects/7362' title='Odd Fellows'>odd fellows</a> meeting.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> except <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>.  I went two.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We walked and Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> come after us in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>machine</a>.  Henry went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and played with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/326' title='Fred Hutcherson'>Fred</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/327' title='Irvin Hutcherson'>Irvin Hutcherson</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Today was <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denias</a> birthday.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I would of liked to seen <span class='line-break'> </span> her.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-495">
<h3><a name="page-495">Monday, April 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> in <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  Marvin went as far <span class='line-break'> </span> as <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I staid at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I killed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie<span class='line-break'> </span> Craddock</a> come this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to see <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-496">
<h3><a name="page-496">Tuesday, April 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> did not hang out the clothes.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She put in a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and we quilted <span class='line-break'> </span> some.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone this evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> was most passed <span class='line-break'> </span> fording.  He come home and <span class='line-break'> </span> helped me <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milk</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss</a> come and bought <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> this evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-497">
<h3><a name="page-497">Wednesday, May  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed some this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and scrubbed the kitc<a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>hen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> floor this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William</a> built fire <span class='line-break'> </span> boxes in the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight a dog passed <span class='line-break'> </span> and in a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> and several <span class='line-break'> </span> other men come and said <span class='line-break'> </span> that the dog was <a href='../subjects/447' title='rabies'>mad</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some one killed him over <span class='line-break'> </span> near <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-498">
<h3><a name="page-498">Thursday, May  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on their <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie</a> and <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie<span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all come to help <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> q<span class='line-break'> </span> uilt.  We finished the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and I and all the <span class='line-break'> </span> children went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while late this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/80' title='Ludy Pugh'>Ludy Pugh</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben got one from <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John<span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-499">
<h3><a name="page-499">Friday, May  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Had turnip <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/284' title='salad'>salet</a> for dinner the <span class='line-break'> </span> last that we will get this <span class='line-break'> </span> spring I expect.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We heard that the <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Edmons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> boys <a href='../subjects/447' title='rabies'>killed their dogs</a><span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I know they was sorry <span class='line-break'> </span> to have it to do.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> to <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-500">
<h3><a name="page-500">Saturday, May  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> come over here this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I went [with] her to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben.  We come by the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant <span class='line-break'> </span> beds</a> and got a few <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a> plants.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had early <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and all went to the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school<span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> folks <span class='line-break'> </span> come down and gave a <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for the benefit of the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/389' title='Red Cross'>Red Cross</a>.  There was a <span class='line-break'> </span> big crowd there.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-501">
<h3><a name="page-501">Sunday, May  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> family staid at home all <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  I was at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> has <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>a little girl</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was at Marvins.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They sent <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> over to <span class='line-break'> </span> Kates this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She will take care of <span class='line-break'> </span> her a few days.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-502">
<h3><a name="page-502">Monday, May  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hauled manure this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and eat dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Rubin</a> brought me home on <span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  I thank them <span class='line-break'> </span> for every kindness shown to poor <span class='line-break'> </span> me.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> staid <span class='line-break'> </span> here some today with <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>.  They have such good <span class='line-break'> </span> times.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-503">
<h3><a name="page-503">Tuesday, May  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> some.  Ben plowed <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <a href='../subjects/452' title='Ernest Lovelace'>Ernest Lovelace</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> staid <span class='line-break'> </span> here nearly all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They all did so well that we <span class='line-break'> </span> enjoy having them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went and bathed <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>the <span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> come this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and got a <a href='../subjects/453' title='pig'>pig</a>.  He paid $7.00 <span class='line-break'> </span> for it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> come here <span class='line-break'> </span> today and went to work.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He thinks he will make <span class='line-break'> </span> a crop of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I hope he may stay and <span class='line-break'> </span> do well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-504">
<h3><a name="page-504">Wednesday, May  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/455' title='weeding'>pulled weeds</a> out of the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant <span class='line-break'> </span> bed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I chopped some in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and a round the <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin sent his <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> down <span class='line-break'> </span> here to day.  Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie Brumfield</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> staid here <span class='line-break'> </span> all day to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-505">
<h3><a name="page-505">Thursday, May  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to try and get a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to plow a few days.  Did not get <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and bathed <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>the baby</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> After <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Children and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Carries.  I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> Planted some <a href='../subjects/456' title='gourds'>gourd</a> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-506">
<h3><a name="page-506">Friday, May 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day until near <span class='line-break'> </span> night there was a <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> cloud and <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> a little <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> and dressed <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7654' title='Eva Smith'>the baby</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/7943' title='Mamie Hutcherson'>Mrs John Hutcherson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come and all the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The first time she come on a <span class='line-break'> </span> visit this year.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to Carries a <span class='line-break'> </span> gain this evening.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We are talking of going to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-507">
<h3><a name="page-507">Saturday, May 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Just at night <span class='line-break'> </span> we had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> fixed up the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried me and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fished</a> but did not catch <span class='line-break'> </span> anything.  <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Paul to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that he did.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-508">
<h3><a name="page-508">Sunday, May 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim Powers</a> and spent <span class='line-break'> </span> the day.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the day went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was there.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> brought <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We now intend starting to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> in the morning <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> and I.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-509">
<h3><a name="page-509">Monday, May 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning rain <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> brought <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We staid at <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> until after three oclock <span class='line-break'> </span> then come to <a href='../subjects/7214' title='Petersburg, Virginia'>Peters Burg</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and from there to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> come after us at <span class='line-break'> </span> the depo.  It <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thundered</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> all the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some young man helped us <span class='line-break'> </span> with our suitcases <span class='line-break'> </span> I will remember him <span class='line-break'> </span> with pleasure.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-510">
<h3><a name="page-510">Tuesday, May 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> morning <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> and [I] went <span class='line-break'> </span> in town this evening.  Went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see the <a href='../subjects/461' title='movies'>moving pictures</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We went a gain <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> and <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with us.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I think <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> mighty pretty place. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We went in the green <span class='line-break'> </span> house and looked a round.  <span class='line-break'> </span> There is lots of pretty plants <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This is wrote May the 15th in <span class='line-break'> </span> the morning before <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-511">
<h3><a name="page-511">Wednesday, May 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day done nothing<span class='line-break'> </span> all morning<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> and three children<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and I went went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/462' title='College Hill Park'>College Hill Park</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and saw a merry go around<span class='line-break'> </span> and dip to dip.  Will and<span class='line-break'> </span> the children rode a round<span class='line-break'> </span> I don't like to look at <span class='line-break'> </span> them. We are all at <span class='line-break'> </span> Willies to night<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-512">
<h3><a name="page-512">Thursday, May 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I are at <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willies</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Went down town early and <span class='line-break'> </span> Mollie bought some things <span class='line-break'> </span> then we started for the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/463' title='boat'>boat</a>.  Went on <a href='../subjects/464' title='street car'>street car</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a mile or so then <span class='line-break'> </span> on the boat.  Eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and had a berth.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> and <a href='../subjects/466' title='steak'>steak</a> <a href='../subjects/467' title='cauliflower'>cauiflowers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/468' title='lettuce'>lettuce</a> salid <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> supper.  Was all night <span class='line-break'> </span> and until seven next <span class='line-break'> </span> morning getting to <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmouth</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This wrote the 17th.  I could <span class='line-break'> </span> not find a pen or pencil <span class='line-break'> </span> last night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-513">
<h3><a name="page-513">Friday, May 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  Come off <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/463' title='boat'>boat</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/7215' title='William Brumfield'>Willie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> left us at landing.  <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> met us and went <span class='line-break'> </span> with us to <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howard Fergersons</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We eat <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> and <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> Fergersons then went to <a href='../subjects/7775' title='Virginia Beach, Virginia'>Va Beach</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7776' title='Cape Henry, Virginia'>Cape Henry</a>.  Saw lots of <span class='line-break'> </span> things new to us.  Fergersons <span class='line-break'> </span> went with us to night.  Three <span class='line-break'> </span> ladies <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julias</a> friends come <span class='line-break'> </span> also <a href='../subjects/7771' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield (b 1878)'>Henry Brumfield</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had a pleasant time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This is wrote Sat morning.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-514">
<h3><a name="page-514">Saturday, May 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy this morning <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  We went to <a href='../subjects/7693' title='Newport News, Virginia'>New <span class='line-break'> </span> Port News</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Crossed on the <a href='../subjects/463' title='boat'>boat</a> twice <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7777' title='Hampton Roads'>Hampton Roads</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> could not see the <a href='../subjects/7778' title='aviators'>aviators</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> after we went.  They were <span class='line-break'> </span> not flying this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We certainly did go a <span class='line-break'> </span> round.  I have seen <span class='line-break'> </span> more than I ever expected <span class='line-break'> </span> to see.  Guess it will <span class='line-break'> </span> be the last time that <span class='line-break'> </span> I will ever see down <span class='line-break'> </span> here a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-515">
<h3><a name="page-515">Sunday, May 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I come home to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> and Robert and <span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia met Mollie.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> met me.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> made the trip from <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmouth</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> home all right.  <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howard <span class='line-break'> </span> Ferguson</a> come with us to <span class='line-break'> </span> the depot.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> and Howard <span class='line-break'> </span> was just as nice to us as <span class='line-break'> </span> they could be.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I found them all as well <span class='line-break'> </span> as usual.  Had two <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to come fresh while I was <span class='line-break'> </span> gone.  I have bin well <span class='line-break'> </span> while I was gone.  To night <span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>tooth hurts</a> me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-516">
<h3><a name="page-516">Monday, May 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> Put ashes on the <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made her <a href='../subjects/9095' title='waist'>silk waist</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.   The <a href='../subjects/7220' title='preacher'>preacher</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see Paul this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-517">
<h3><a name="page-517">Tuesday, May 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and I and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Jessie Worshams pond</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>caught some minners</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> When I got home Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> had <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and she got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-518">
<h3><a name="page-518">Wednesday, May 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a> to day now <span class='line-break'> </span> he is ready for rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a> come this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and staid a few hours.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> come here <span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  She made <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> two shirts to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I both had a <span class='line-break'> </span> hand in the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> two rows of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got one doz aster plants <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie Brumfield</a> sent <span class='line-break'> </span> them from <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-519">
<h3><a name="page-519">Thursday, May 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7225' title='Steven Davis'>Stevin Davis s</a> to day and <span class='line-break'> </span> got a sack of <a href='../subjects/253' title='fertilizer'>ferterlizer</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Finished <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Pauls</a> <a href='../subjects/7221' title='tobacco land'>tobacco land</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> bottom.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I planted <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7226' title='peanuts'>pea nuts</a>.  I planted some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>Irish potatoes</a>.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> made <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried Alma to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> all went.  I washed dishes <span class='line-break'> </span> while they were gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-520">
<h3><a name="page-520">Friday, May 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We had a <span class='line-break'> </span> good <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> last night.  We <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> all day.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> planted and <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> drawed plants.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some men come to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> about a <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben put the <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> in a <a href='../subjects/7227' title='pigpen'>pen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> last night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-521">
<h3><a name="page-521">Saturday, May 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The menfolks <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> helped them <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to Blairs this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and got <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe slips</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and I drawed <span class='line-break'> </span> plants part of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> solde her <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day we guess.  She passed <span class='line-break'> </span> here some one driving her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-522">
<h3><a name="page-522">Sunday, May 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  I got a snack <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  After dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr</a> and <a href='../subjects/8093' title='Melissa Mayhew'>Mrs Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come.  Ben and Mr Mayhew <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>played croquet</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7302' title='Mrs Rice'>Mrs Rice</a> home this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> home to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George <span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a> for dinner from <span class='line-break'> </span> preaching.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-523">
<h3><a name="page-523">Monday, May 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> drawed plants.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> In the evening Josie went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/238' title='plantbeds'>plant bed</a>.  I planted <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe slips</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a lot of hard <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> this evening but no <span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-524">
<h3><a name="page-524">Tuesday, May 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We want <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> badly.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> all went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> finished planting <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoe <span class='line-break'> </span> slips</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> Bennett <span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening. <span class='line-break'> </span> We all went up to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a while.  <a href='../subjects/7230' title='Mr and Mrs Padget'>Mr and Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Padget</a> and <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel Worsham</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla Blair</a> was at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/367' title='Odie Kellie'>Odie Kellies</a> after the <a href='../subjects/7232' title='tobacco planter'>tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> planter</a>.  He carried all the <span class='line-break'> </span> children with him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-525">
<h3><a name="page-525">Wednesday, May 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">

<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We carried <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> and we went <span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come and got a <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-526">
<h3><a name="page-526">Thursday, May 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <span class='line-break'> </span> hot.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> commenced to plow <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I capped some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie preserved them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Paul killed two <a href='../subjects/7235' title='squirrels'>squirrels</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We had them <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7236' title='Walter Layne'>Walter Layne</a> come this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening to look at my <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a>.  He said he would <span class='line-break'> </span> come in the morning and get <span class='line-break'> </span> her.  Josie and I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a>.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> Christenia was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9: o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-527">
<h3><a name="page-527">Friday, May 31, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with a planter.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> droped plants.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7238' title='Mr Murphy'>Mr Murphy</a> come to see <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout getting the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'> school <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> for a <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>

<div id="page-528">
<h3><a name="page-528">Saturday, June  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>. Got <span class='line-break'> </span> done a while before night <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to Cedar Forest. <span class='line-break'> </span> Carried some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> The men went <a href='../subjects/309' title='bathing'>bathing</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> went with them to the store. <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7435' title='Jesse Worsham'>Mr Jessie <span class='line-break'> </span> Worshams</a> Mill Pond to fish. <span class='line-break'> </span> None of us caught any <span class='line-break'> </span> thing to keep. Cordie and Isla <span class='line-break'> </span> caught a fish a peice but <span class='line-break'> </span> did not get them out of the <span class='line-break'> </span> pond. <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> to day. <a href='../subjects/301' title='Frank Blair'>Frank</a> and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George</a> went to Danville <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 15 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and two of the <span class='line-break'> </span> children <span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; Josie has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>School House</a> to a play.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-529">
<h3><a name="page-529">Sunday, June  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> family went to visit <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> Power</a> and family.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home until <span class='line-break'> </span> evening then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate <span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> was there and some <span class='line-break'> </span> of the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin carried them home <span class='line-break'> </span> and then brough me home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come with us did <span class='line-break'> </span> not get out of the car.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin to <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and then to Blairs.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>

</div>
</div>

<div id="page-530">
<h3><a name="page-530">Monday, June  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this morning<span class='line-break'> </span> it was badly needed.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> was at <span class='line-break'> </span> his brothers near <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He brought a <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> home <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/399' title='Mrs Bailiss'>Mrs Bailiss</a> come and got <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.  I worked in <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/7241' title='Eula Mayhew'>Eula Mayhew</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> and got a few <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomato plants</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josies</a> <a href='../subjects/7242' title='carding'>cards</a> to make <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/328' title='bats'>bats</a> for a <a href='../subjects/8' title='quilting'>quilt</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-531">
<h3><a name="page-531">Tuesday, June  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then commence to work out <span class='line-break'> </span> the tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Killed the first young <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come to Carries.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come here,  They wanted <span class='line-break'> </span> my <a href='../subjects/7244' title='suitcase'>suitcase</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  Hope she may <span class='line-break'> </span> be better by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-532">
<h3><a name="page-532">Wednesday, June  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> found a swarm of <a href='../subjects/7245' title='bees'>bees</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/7246' title='orchard'>orchard</a> yesterday.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben hived them this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope that they may do well.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I worked <span class='line-break'> </span> some in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  Planted <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7247' title='muskmelon'>muskmellon seed</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> few <a href='../subjects/7226' title='peanuts'>pea nuts</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/7248' title='pumpkins'>pumpkin seed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to Blairs late <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  They were all <span class='line-break'> </span> well.  <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie Blair</a> was there. <span class='line-break'> </span> Did not see <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> or <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> They were at <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-533">
<h3><a name="page-533">Thursday, June  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day most of the day. <span class='line-break'> </span> Had a little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> still <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>working <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumber</a> and <a href='../subjects/7251' title='pumpkin'>pumpkin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this evening and <span class='line-break'> </span> got some things.  Among them <span class='line-break'> </span> were 4 tin <a href='../subjects/7252' title='buckets'>buckets</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mr <a href='../subjects/7253' title='Dave Layne'>Dave Layne</a> and his son [ink smear] <span class='line-break'> </span> Walter and got a <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> [smear] <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> are <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  If anyone wonders why <span class='line-break'> </span> this page is so blotted, I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-534">
<h3><a name="page-534">Friday, June  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  I washed a little <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/77' title='baking'>Baked</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>. This evening she washed <span class='line-break'> </span> the dining room floor.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7255' title='George Worsham'>George Worsham</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> assessing property.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <a href='../subjects/7256' title='sunflowers'>sunflower</a> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to try and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mend</a> the <a href='../subjects/7257' title='freezer'>freezer</a>.  Hope <span class='line-break'> </span> he can get it <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-535">
<h3><a name="page-535">Saturday, June  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Cool for the <span class='line-break'> </span> time of year.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> worked until <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/7362' title='Odd Fellows'>Odd<span class='line-break'> </span> fellows</a> had a lecture this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> and the ladies solde <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice<span class='line-break'> </span> cream</a>.  There was a big <span class='line-break'> </span> crowd there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> brough cream home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie went up there <span class='line-break'> </span> and got some.  She did not <span class='line-break'> </span> want to go.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went back to Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone tonight.  We expect <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7258' title='Mr Turner'>Mr Turner</a> to come with <span class='line-break'> </span> him home.  Josie is upstairs <span class='line-break'> </span> preparing a room for him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-536">
<h3><a name="page-536">Sunday, June  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7258' title='Mr Turner'>Mr Turner</a> staid here last <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  I like what I know of <span class='line-break'> </span> him fine.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7259' title='Whittles Depot, Virginia'>Whittles</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> Mr Turner to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Ben and family and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  They had a lot <span class='line-break'> </span> of company.  <a href='../subjects/269' title='Earnest Craddock'>Earnest</a> and <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie Bennett</a> come while I <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel</a> and <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Wren</a> and family <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  To night Ben has <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a>.  Hope he will <span class='line-break'> </span> be better by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-537">
<h3><a name="page-537">Monday, June 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
