<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> He cut his <a href='../subjects/7261' title='rye'>rye</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> come home at <span class='line-break'> </span> twelve oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Paul carried <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children and I up to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We went to see <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag Brumfield</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> and <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7262' title='Charlottesville, Virginia'>Charlottesville</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day to see <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> married.  <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> and <a href='../subjects/7223' title='Howard Ferguson'>Howard <span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> come to Reynolds <span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-538">
<h3><a name="page-538">Tuesday, June 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day we need <span class='line-break'> </span> rain so bad.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>worked tobacco</a> half <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day then cut <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and then worked the <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet <span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/7226' title='peanuts'>pea nuts</a> <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I got up <span class='line-break'> </span> some of the <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> all the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> got <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazels</a> <a href='../subjects/7266' title='photography'>pictures</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  She is not pleased <span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  I am anxious <span class='line-break'> </span> to see them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-539">
<h3><a name="page-539">Wednesday, June 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Clear most of the day<span class='line-break'> </span>  a sprinkle of <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The men finished <a href='../subjects/7249' title='working tobacco'>workin over <span class='line-break'> </span> their tobacco</a> to day and cut <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and [I] washed to day <span class='line-break'> </span> and then got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and Josie and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7267' title='Mount Airy, Virginia'>Mount <span class='line-break'> </span> Airy</a> to night to an <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice <span class='line-break'> </span> cream</a> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7268' title='Nat Wooding'>Nat Woodings</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> broke <span class='line-break'> </span> down to day he was at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Mr Edmons</a>.  Ben let him <span class='line-break'> </span> have his to make his <span class='line-break'> </span> round on.  He brought it <span class='line-break'> </span> back be fore night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-540">
<h3><a name="page-540">Thursday, June 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> cutting <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> come a while <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and two of <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> children <span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Lee was looking <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/7269' title='tobacco plants'>tobacco plants</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> before <span class='line-break'> </span> night today and Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> all went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and have not got back <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-541">
<h3><a name="page-541">Friday, June 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cut<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home and worked <span class='line-break'> </span> hard all day.  To night she <span class='line-break'> </span> is very much <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> her mouth and jaw hurting.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> carried <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie <span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7435' title='Jesse Worsham'>Mr Jess W</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> pond.  We did not <a href='../subjects/9093' title='fishing'>catch any<span class='line-break'> </span> thing</a>.  I bough a <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> that <span class='line-break'> </span> a col woman caught.  It was <span class='line-break'> </span> a fine one.  We come back <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout twelve.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I stoped at <a href='../subjects/7271' title='W Wooding'>Mr W Woodings</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/8608' title='Mr Bookers'>Bookers</a> tryed to get <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7273' title='pineapple'>grated pine apple</a>.  Could not <span class='line-break'> </span> get it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben tonight is at Powers.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-542">
<h3><a name="page-542">Saturday, June 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cut<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> at <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Power</a> brought to[sic] <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7274' title='reaper'>reaper</a> home to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> worked on the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> til noon.  Then he <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> after <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a>.  The ladies of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> neighborhood sold <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a> at the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Miss Fannie <span class='line-break'> </span> Power</a> come with Ben.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They are all gone to the <span class='line-break'> </span> school house now.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> worked hard all <span class='line-break'> </span> day fixin her cream <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a>.  I do hope <span class='line-break'> </span> they may have luck <span class='line-break'> </span> and sell their cream.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss</a> come here this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  His <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> got cut <span class='line-break'> </span> in the wire.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-543">
<h3><a name="page-543">Sunday, June 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Miss Fannie <span class='line-break'> </span> Power</a> staid here last night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss's</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and sewed up <span class='line-break'> </span> a cut on his <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Robert Hubbards</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Fannie went home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid home by my self <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All at home and a bed <span class='line-break'> </span> now.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They were not at home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-544">
<h3><a name="page-544">Monday, June 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>We had a good <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning it was badly<span class='line-break'> </span> needed.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> day after it quit raining.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> over to the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a> to get the things <span class='line-break'> </span> that was left Sat night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I worked a little in <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went up to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come with her back.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owens</a> sent us a <span class='line-break'> </span> mess of <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-545">
<h3><a name="page-545">Tuesday, June 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> then they <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> gave us some <a href='../subjects/7278' title='scrapple'>scraple</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> so she knowed what to cook.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I washed a few things this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> wash some <a href='../subjects/7279' title='guano sacks'>guano sacks</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished getting up the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7265' title='onions'>onions</a> this evening.  Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> and I thinned the corn <span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a>.  <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> brought a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> for Josie to <span class='line-break'> </span> make this week.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-546">
<h3><a name="page-546">Wednesday, June 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy but no rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> hauled up <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. I <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie</a> and [ink smudge] <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> will spend the night <span class='line-break'> </span> here.  I when see <span class='line-break'> </span> that I cover[unclear]  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Done the 19th I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> sleep last night and did <span class='line-break'> </span> not finish my writing and <span class='line-break'> </span> dropped a drop of <a href='../subjects/436' title='ink'>ink</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-547">
<h3><a name="page-547">Thursday, June 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> finished getting up <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7261' title='rye'>rye</a> this morning.  Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7280' title='Hubbards'>Hubbards</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7281' title='the river'>the river</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  Caught <a href='../subjects/7282' title='eels'>eels</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Got home at dark.  Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> had <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> and got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad.  I was tired.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.  I am glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> hear from them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-548">
<h3><a name="page-548">Friday, June 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Had a good <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/437' title='chinking'>chinked</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We set <span class='line-break'> </span> by a <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some things <span class='line-break'> </span> that we had put off.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have not seen any of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> people to day or <span class='line-break'> </span> heard from them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Paul has gone to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> to night <span class='line-break'> </span> to the rehersal of a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-549">
<h3><a name="page-549">Saturday, June 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> and <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> Had a good <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> last night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> thinned <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> meeting of the <a href='../subjects/221' title='school board'>School Board</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> caught several fish.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>Lodge</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul has gone to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> the rest of <span class='line-break'> </span> them has gone to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-550">
<h3><a name="page-550">Sunday, June 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> day for this time <span class='line-break'> </span> of the year.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I staid at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Gladis and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin <span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come.  They were here <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that Kate come.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> not bin here in a long <span class='line-break'> </span> time be fore.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a>s <span class='line-break'> </span> to an <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a> <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The cream was fine I <span class='line-break'> </span> did enjoy it so much.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> come home on <a href='../subjects/7283' title='Bob Starkey'>Mr Bob <span class='line-break'> </span> Starkeys</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> was glad of the <span class='line-break'> </span> ride.  Heard that <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nannie <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> has <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>a girl</a> born <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-551">
<h3><a name="page-551">Monday, June 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cut <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got the <span class='line-break'> </span> floors washed by <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Josie and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> gave me some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> come here but <span class='line-break'> </span> no one was at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am very sorry.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-552">
<h3><a name="page-552">Tuesday, June 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> half the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and worked some <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7284' title='Ellen Bailiss'>Ellen</a> and <a href='../subjects/7285' title='Melvin Bailiss'>Melvin Bailiss</a>  <span class='line-break'> </span> come and got <a href='../subjects/7286' title='milk'>milk</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> to <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard this morning that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7287' title='Sam Carter'>Sam Carter</a> was to be <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-553">
<h3><a name="page-553">Wednesday, June 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day no rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>replanted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  She carried <span class='line-break'> </span> the children with her to <span class='line-break'> </span> Renan.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar <span class='line-break'> </span> Forest</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  I caught <span class='line-break'> </span> three <a href='../subjects/7288' title='catfish'>cat fish</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Turned them in the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>branch</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> has gone to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-554">
<h3><a name="page-554">Thursday, June 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> and <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar <span class='line-break'> </span> Forest</a> hunting <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> to sow.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He got some from <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee B</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washing <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posey Reynolds</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>the new baby</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a house full <span class='line-break'> </span> of company there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Did not see <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds she was gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thompsons</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We bough war stamps <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/242' title='Irvin Lewis'>Irvin Lewis</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7290' title='Tom Starkey'>Tom Starkey</a> come by <span class='line-break'> </span> here on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> brough me home from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7291' title='Johnson&apos;s barn'>Johnson's barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> has gone to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> a gain <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-555">
<h3><a name="page-555">Friday, June 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>did not catch many</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> plowed <span class='line-break'> </span> while he carried us.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> walked as far as <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thompsons</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> went with Paul to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> brought me some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> am glad of them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> All of the children <span class='line-break'> </span> are a sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-556">
<h3><a name="page-556">Saturday, June 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> cut <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She baked <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and fixed for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at Stanton High School.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They will be a <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> there <span class='line-break'> </span> to night by some of the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan crowd</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went a bout 2 in <span class='line-break'> </span> the evening.  I hope that <span class='line-break'> </span> they may make good.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> proceeds will go to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/389' title='Red Cross'>Red Cross</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-557">
<h3><a name="page-557">Sunday, June 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> staid here and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben brough <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> from <a href='../subjects/7293' title='Mr Thompson'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Thompsons</a>.  Josie made <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and all <span class='line-break'> </span> the children come and <span class='line-break'> </span> brought <a href='../subjects/54' title='custard'>custard</a> ready for <span class='line-break'> </span> freezin.  The[y] made two <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7257' title='freezer'>freezers</a> full.  It was all <span class='line-break'> </span> good and we all enjoyed <span class='line-break'> </span> it so much.  While <span class='line-break'> </span> we were eating <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Dews</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/7559' title='Board Dews'>Board Dews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all come.  We had a <span class='line-break'> </span> plenty for them all.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some of them played <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>croquet</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-558">
<h3><a name="page-558">Monday, July  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> in the night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Clear to day and <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> blowin.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She cooked <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> made <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> the ice.  Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7295' title='laying by'>laying by</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Bens and commenced on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a>.  Josie went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nannie Reynolds</a> and <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>the <span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a>.  Went over to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7297' title='Virginia Owen?'>Virginia</a> and <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> come this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The children and I <span class='line-break'> </span> chopped the grass out <span class='line-break'> </span> of the path this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-559">
<h3><a name="page-559">Tuesday, July  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good bright day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men folks <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> got up <span class='line-break'> </span> hay.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/7298' title='Mrs Winston'>Mrs Winston</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/73' title='Hattie Gilbert'>Hattie Gilbert</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> gave us a mess of <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  We have got <span class='line-break'> </span> good neighbors.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> walked to Mr Creasys <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> pond.  The <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> is so <span class='line-break'> </span> low that you <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>cant fish</a> in <span class='line-break'> </span> it to catch anything.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We come back by <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She was at home by her <span class='line-break'> </span> self.  <a href='../subjects/7297' title='Virginia Owen?'>Virginia</a> was at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds's</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-560">
<h3><a name="page-560">Wednesday, July  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben plowed the <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet potatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben mowed.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and worked some in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  Josie tried to find <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> found enough for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> with <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>Posies <span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> hope she <span class='line-break'> </span> may get well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Hope he may <span class='line-break'> </span> be able to work by in the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-561">
<h3><a name="page-561">Thursday, July  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> got up <span class='line-break'> </span> hay this evening.  Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> family and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7300' title='Clover Bottom'>Clover Bottom</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/389' title='Red Cross'>Red Cross</a> meeting.  <span class='line-break'> </span> It <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> down there <span class='line-break'> </span> I wish it had of rained <span class='line-break'> </span> here.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> raked <a href='../subjects/7301' title='hay'>hay</a>.  I finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-562">
<h3><a name="page-562">Friday, July  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> stacked <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7292' title='oats'>oats</a> to day and finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> for him self <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a>.  Plowed some <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> most all <span class='line-break'> </span> of it.  I got a new <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> sent it <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening by mail. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p>  I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while and then to <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a>.  I carried <a href='../subjects/7302' title='Mrs Rice'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Rice</a> a <a href='../subjects/119' title='bonnet'>bonnett</a> that <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> made the bonnett.<span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie Smith furnished the <span class='line-break'> </span> material and gave it to <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Rice.  Posie and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>his mother</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was gone to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola (Bennett) Jefferson</a> .  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We are having some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night and need it two.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-563">
<h3><a name="page-563">Saturday, July  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons's</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> most all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Worshams pond</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We come home for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> To night we went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school house</a> to see <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has bin <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-564">
<h3><a name="page-564">Sunday, July  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> work on his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> all the morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They had a lot of company <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and Ben and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> home with them home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> had a <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a> to day.  He went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7304' title='Riceville, Virginia'>Riceville</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> got in the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and eat a lot of it <span class='line-break'> </span> off.  <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> got <span class='line-break'> </span> him out of the corn.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-565">
<h3><a name="page-565">Monday, July  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy and some rain <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> commenced <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7295' title='laying by'>laying by</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7305' title='Mr Hubbard'>Mr Hubbard</a> come to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and commenced to <a href='../subjects/7306' title='well digging'>bore a well</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I dodged <span class='line-break'> </span> a round as usual.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-566">
<h3><a name="page-566">Tuesday, July  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> in their <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed I <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We got the <span class='line-break'> </span> first <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> out of our <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> today and I burnt <span class='line-break'> </span> them so that we could not <span class='line-break'> </span> eat them.  I had <a href='../subjects/296' title='fried chicken'>fried <span class='line-break'> </span> chicken</a> and that was all.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  Very much <span class='line-break'> </span> a gainst his will.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I caught enough <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to make a dish for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Mr <a href='../subjects/7307' title='Carrington Hubbard'>Carrington Hubbard</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was here a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I did not meet <span class='line-break'> </span> him [ink mark] Well I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> sleep and made my <span class='line-break'> </span> mark.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-567">
<h3><a name="page-567">Wednesday, July 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Had a sprinkle <span class='line-break'> </span> of rain this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> picked <a href='../subjects/7299' title='black berries'>black berries</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and made <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> had his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrashed</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped.  They thrashed <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I helped <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> get <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day is better <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-568">
<h3><a name="page-568">Thursday, July 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7309' title='Hutchersons'>Hutchersons</a> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrashed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> here to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and got <span class='line-break'> </span> the most of <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I cant find my <span class='line-break'> </span> glasses to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Am writing by <span class='line-break'> </span> guess.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-569">
<h3><a name="page-569">Friday, July 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve oclock <span class='line-break'> </span> then went with <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom <span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a> to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> When the cloud came up we <span class='line-break'> </span> stopped at <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thompsons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> found them all well.  Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> gave me <a href='../subjects/3' title='ice'>ice</a> to make <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>cream</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I am a sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-570">
<h3><a name="page-570">Saturday, July 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Need rain yet.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> fix <span class='line-break'> </span> in his <a href='../subjects/7310' title='pump'>pump</a>.  To night <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has gone to Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> came this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> to tell us good by.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> He has got to go to camp <span class='line-break'> </span> Tuesday.  I feel so sorry for <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us.  Tonight <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul and Earl has gone to see <span class='line-break'> </span> some of the young folks.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> gave an <a href='../subjects/55' title='ice cream'>ice cream</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  We were invited did not <span class='line-break'> </span> go.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-571">
<h3><a name="page-571">Sunday, July 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good Day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> home this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> staid all day <span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  Lizzie and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> were there and <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren <span class='line-break'> </span> Worsham</a> and family was <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Josie and Ben come <span class='line-break'> </span> home early.  <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>his mother</a> just now <span class='line-break'> </span> started home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-572">
<h3><a name="page-572">Monday, July 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> did not get any grinding.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> fix his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7310' title='pump'>pump</a> a gain to day.  Helped <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen fix his <a href='../subjects/45' title='stove'>stove</a> pipe.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie Wooding</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made her a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  To night Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> bought <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7311' title='shotgun shells'>shells</a>.  Paul killed two <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7312' title='rabbits'>rabbits</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> sent the <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> home this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see Bens and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Pauls</a> crops this evening.  It <span class='line-break'> </span> looks good now.  We need <span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie has <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>head ache</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope she will soon be <span class='line-break'> </span> well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-573">
<h3><a name="page-573">Tuesday, July 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning rain this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> was there <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.   <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to George <span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> is sick tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin went to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7313' title='Piney Grove'>Piney Grove</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Helped <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Mr Edmons</a> home <span class='line-break'> </span> with his new <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-574">
<h3><a name="page-574">Wednesday, July 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/165' title='horseshoes'>shod</a> his <a href='../subjects/289' title='colt'>colt</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> and got <span class='line-break'> </span> a nice basket of peaches <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> he has gone to up in his <span class='line-break'> </span> olde neighborhood.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and helped Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> peal some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning but is some better <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a note tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-575">
<h3><a name="page-575">Thursday, July 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some rain tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> fix his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7310' title='pump'>pump</a> a gain this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> has not come home <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> did not get his grinding.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went to Cedar <span class='line-break'> </span> Forest and carried <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I with him.  We did not <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> to speak of.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He got his <a href='../subjects/7315' title='flue eyes'>flue eyes</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for the new <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-576">
<h3><a name="page-576">Friday, July 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> today.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> commenced <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>topping</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> home this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Several of <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> children are <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly do hope that <span class='line-break'> </span> they may get well soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> was <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Tuesday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-577">
<h3><a name="page-577">Saturday, July 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> put in <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7315' title='flue eyes'>flue eyes</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> and got flour.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I went with him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The river was up so we <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>could not fish</a>.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/7318' title='Creasey&apos;s pond'>Creaseys pond</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> staid a while then come <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> met us there and brought <span class='line-break'> </span> us home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> here today. The first time <span class='line-break'> </span> in a long time.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come to see <span class='line-break'> </span> us a while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has not come in to<span class='line-break'> </span> night.  He is attending to <span class='line-break'> </span> some of the <a href='../subjects/7319' title='cattle'>cattle</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-578">
<h3><a name="page-578">Sunday, July 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Mr Edmons</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He went with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all of the rest staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> and played with the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the <span class='line-break'> </span> little children come a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> carried the boys home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> gave them to us.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got dinner.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  I have not bin <span class='line-break'> </span> well today.  Hope I may <span class='line-break'> </span> feel better by morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie is playing the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7320' title='piano'>piano</a> and Ben the <a href='../subjects/7321' title='violin'>violin</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-579">
<h3><a name="page-579">Monday, July 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7325' title='barn daubing'>dobed</a> on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim Powers</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> and done what was most <span class='line-break'> </span> needing to be done.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben and Paul and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to the <a href='../subjects/194' title='school house'>school <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come home to finish his <span class='line-break'> </span> crop.  There was several <span class='line-break'> </span> of the boys had to <a href='../subjects/7567' title='World War I'>start <span class='line-break'> </span> to camp</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Franklin went to bed and <span class='line-break'> </span> to sleep did not have a <span class='line-break'> </span> bit of fuss.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-580">
<h3><a name="page-580">Tuesday, July 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day here.  There <span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a> and rain a <span class='line-break'> </span> round and very hard <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.
