This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen helped <a href='../subjects/7323' title='Hutcherson'>Hutcherson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening she put strings <span class='line-break'> </span> around Bens <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water <span class='line-break'> </span> melon</a> patch.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> they were all at home <span class='line-break'> </span> except Johnson.  I had a <span class='line-break'> </span> pleasant visit.  I like <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a> fine.  Come back <span class='line-break'> </span> by <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> they were getting <span class='line-break'> </span> on fine.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-581">
<h3><a name="page-581">Wednesday, July 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley Hutcherson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrash</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> half a day a <span class='line-break'> </span> piece.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> worked on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span> a splendid <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> gave me some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <a href='../subjects/252' title='Mrs Hutcherson'>Mrs Hutcherson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> gave me some nice apples <span class='line-break'> </span> to cook.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-582">
<h3><a name="page-582">Thursday, July 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7325' title='barn daubing'>dobbing</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a>.  The <a href='../subjects/7309' title='Hutchersons'>Hutchersons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> finished <a href='../subjects/7308' title='threshing'>thrashing</a> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> night and <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went with <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George</a> and <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> to <a href='../subjects/7326' title='John Reynolds'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> John Reynolds</a> to see olde <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7327' title='Mrs Blair'>Mrs Blair</a>.  Shes very <span class='line-break'> </span> feeble.  <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> come with <span class='line-break'> </span> us home.  We had a <span class='line-break'> </span> good trip nothing happened <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry brought me home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope I am thankful <span class='line-break'> </span> for all the kindness that <span class='line-break'> </span> is shown me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-583">
<h3><a name="page-583">Friday, July 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>topped tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> to <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>did not catch many</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> fish.  We walked up by <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7328' title='Mr Johnson'>Mr Johnsons</a> house.  <a href='../subjects/7329' title='Mrs Johnson'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Johnson</a> was very nice to us.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> come after us.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and all the children <span class='line-break'> </span> come with him.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> a pleasant evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We got home in good <span class='line-break'> </span> time to <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milk</a> and <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a>.  Josie had <a href='../subjects/7330' title='cornbread'>corn <span class='line-break'> </span> batter bread</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> and we did enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-584">
<h3><a name="page-584">Saturday, July 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> has had holiday most <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> and his boys <span class='line-break'> </span> come up here and played <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>croquet</a> all of the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some of the Mayhew <span class='line-break'> </span> children and some of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> come to play with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a>.  <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> come a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I think they had a good <span class='line-break'> </span> time.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We cooked <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/236' title='cabbage'>cabbage</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben and Mayhew <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>Lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-585">
<h3><a name="page-585">Sunday, July 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>played croquet</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and has not got home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-586">
<h3><a name="page-586">Monday, July 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>topped tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Paul <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a> and <a href='../subjects/7332' title='Grit, Virginia'>Grit</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane Reynolds</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She was <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse back</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I think she is a good little <span class='line-break'> </span> woman.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-587">
<h3><a name="page-587">Tuesday, July 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this morning.  A good <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  Had <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> the first from our <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Dews</a> and <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> played <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>croquet</a> all the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a while <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> come by <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They had carried one of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7648' title='A. J. Harvey'>A J Harveys</a> girls to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7293' title='Mr Thompson'>Mr Thompsons</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-588">
<h3><a name="page-588">Wednesday, July 31, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7316' title='topping'>topped tobacco</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> while today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> made a stew and had <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7336' title='cymblins'>cymblins</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all good.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.  We all went <span class='line-break'> </span> and looked at the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then to the <a href='../subjects/7337' title='tobacco ground'>tobacco ground</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to see the <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7339' title='bean patch'>bean patch</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.  Their <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> to <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evylin <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have fixed some <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night for <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> [scratchy ink blots] <span class='line-break'> </span> I guess I have the meanest <span class='line-break'> </span> pen about here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 : oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-589">
<h3><a name="page-589">Thursday, August  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked getting <a href='../subjects/7340' title='tobacco sticks'>tobacco sticks</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> they went to <a href='../subjects/7211' title='Cedar Forest, Virginia'>Cedar Forest</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/7341' title='flues'>flues</a>.  Got two sets cost <span class='line-break'> </span> $44 got home with them <span class='line-break'> </span> OK.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  This evening <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a> did not <span class='line-break'> </span> catch anything.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fanny Emerson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> is here.  I was glad to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Fanny.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-590">
<h3><a name="page-590">Friday, August  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pulled leaves</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William <span class='line-break'> </span> Gilbert (col)</a> helped them.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Nearly all the children <span class='line-break'> </span> that was big enough <a href='../subjects/7344' title='handing'>handed <span class='line-break'> </span> leaves</a>.  This evening <a href='../subjects/7921' title='Fannie Emerson'>Fanny <span class='line-break'> </span> Emerson</a> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I helped some.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She cooked <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a> and <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> sent <span class='line-break'> </span> her the corn.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Paul and Fanny <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to meeting at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7346' title='Saint John&apos;s Episcopal Church'>St. Johns</a>.  (ink smear)  Well I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> sleep I made my mark.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10:15</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-591">
<h3><a name="page-591">Saturday, August  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks filled a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/7344' title='handing'>handed</a> leaves <span class='line-break'> </span> nearly all day.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Fanny helped <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Fanny went to <span class='line-break'> </span> Mr <a href='../subjects/7348' title='George Emerson'>George Emersons</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried her <span class='line-break'> </span> on the <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evelyn</a> come today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that they come.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> to day saying <span class='line-break'> </span> that she will come to see us <span class='line-break'> </span> soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-592">
<h3><a name="page-592">Sunday, August  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> spend a good part <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> brough me <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He went home for dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7351' title='Alvin Farmer'>Alvin Farmer</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> to see Irvin.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim and <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evelyn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went home this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben carried them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola</a> and <a href='../subjects/7352' title='Faber Jefferson'>Faber <span class='line-break'> </span> Jefferson</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all come over here this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> come by <a href='../subjects/7353' title='Tim Bennett'>Tim Bennetts</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and got some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am very glad of <span class='line-break'> </span> them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-593">
<h3><a name="page-593">Monday, August  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I do[d]ged a <span class='line-break'> </span> round as usual.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening we went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> here and then to Marvins.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin had <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the first I have seen this <span class='line-break'> </span> year.  Josie come by the <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> field and got <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> a basket of <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard this morning that <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia <span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>has a daughter</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> born the 4th.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> and <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-594">
<h3><a name="page-594">Tuesday, August  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> day and very <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>curing</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> did not get his grinding.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed the <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> dishes and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and washed the dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> dishes and ironed most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I got breakfast and <span class='line-break'> </span> called them to eat then <span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> three <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> and watered <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> at three different places <span class='line-break'> </span> then I gathered some <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter <span class='line-break'> </span> beans</a> and helped to <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shell</a> them.  Then <span class='line-break'> </span> fixed the milk ready to churn <span class='line-break'> </span> then <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> a bucket of <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumbers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> fixed to wash some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> After dinner I washed a bout <span class='line-break'> </span> 40 garments then put the <span class='line-break'> </span> cucumbers in brine and salted the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a> and fixed it ready for use.  Then <span class='line-break'> </span> rested a while then milked eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> helped wash dishes and ready to go to bed.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-595">
<h3><a name="page-595">Wednesday, August  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> day some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a> and <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> but no rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed and hemed the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7356' title='curtains'>curtains</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pull leaves</a> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> and got some nice <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Will have them to put up in <span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  I am very glad <span class='line-break'> </span> of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-596">
<h3><a name="page-596">Thursday, August  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> hot day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> save <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <a href='../subjects/7344' title='handing'>handed</a> leaves <span class='line-break'> </span> and Josie <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We pealed <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> that <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> give us.  Had <a href='../subjects/7358' title='peaches and cream'>peaches and <span class='line-break'> </span> cream</a> for dinner and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> cooked good and I did <span class='line-break'> </span> enjoy my dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Talked with <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night over the <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She said that <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> going to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  I certainly do <span class='line-break'> </span> hope she may have a good <span class='line-break'> </span> time and [be] benifited by <span class='line-break'> </span> going.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-597">
<h3><a name="page-597">Friday, August  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We are having some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night and <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a>.  I do hope <span class='line-break'> </span> that we wont have a <a href='../subjects/82' title='storm'>storm</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I know that God is able to <span class='line-break'> </span> cause it not to be so bad.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The men helped <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a> all day and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I helped this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> all the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> started to <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope that they had a good <span class='line-break'> </span> trip.  Josie got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> saying that <span class='line-break'> </span> she would not come here until <span class='line-break'> </span> September.  We look for <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> tomorrow hope that <span class='line-break'> </span> they may come.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-598">
<h3><a name="page-598">Saturday, August 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> morning.  Some <span class='line-break'> </span> rain this evening and I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7359' title='Mr Baily'>Mr  Baily</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come.  He eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> here.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Baily went to <a href='../subjects/7360' title='Finch'>Finches</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> to meet <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia Brumfield</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and got dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7362' title='Odd Fellows'>odd Fellows</a> <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>Lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-599">
<h3><a name="page-599">Sunday, August 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds <span class='line-break'> </span> a round this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> but no rain here.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home to day <span class='line-break'> </span> until about night. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> and <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> [went] to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a>.  <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> come.  Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> them <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>played croquet</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Carrie and the children come a few minutes.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> brought them on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> brother come <span class='line-break'> </span> to see him this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got the first <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7363' title='corn field'>corn field</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-600">
<h3><a name="page-600">Monday, August 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout this evening but no <span class='line-break'> </span> rain here.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> suckered <span class='line-break'> </span> four rows this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went with him.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> staid longer than Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> thought he would have <span class='line-break'> </span> to stay.  We eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7558' title='Jane Wooding'>Mrs Woodings</a>.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> a good plain dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mr <a href='../subjects/7365' title='John Baily'>John</a> and <a href='../subjects/7366' title='Willie Baily'>Willie Baily</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7367' title='Mrs Hines'>Mrs Hines</a> come with <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben as far as their home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> gathered some <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We picked them off <span class='line-break'> </span> the stems to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> sent over and got <span class='line-break'> </span> some grapes.  <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a> and <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come.  I saw <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie</a> at Chatham.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-601">
<h3><a name="page-601">Tuesday, August 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a>.  Ben and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> and Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> at twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> staid a few minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and Thelma washed <span class='line-break'> </span> some this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and boiled <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7368' title='grapes'>grapes</a>.  Josie <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>put up 14 <span class='line-break'> </span> quarts</a> of <a href='../subjects/7372' title='grape juice'>grape juice</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We gathered and picked <span class='line-break'> </span> off some grapes this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening and to night <span class='line-break'> </span> Thelma and Paul both <span class='line-break'> </span> picked til we finished.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-602">
<h3><a name="page-602">Wednesday, August 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and very hot.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The men folks <a href='../subjects/7894' title='pulling leaves'>pulled leaves</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> them.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I helped.  <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped some two.  Thelma went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> is here.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> with the babies.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I made some <a href='../subjects/7373' title='jelly'>jellie</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Josie <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7372' title='grape juice'>grape juice</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Julia and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> is on a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7374' title='pallet'>pallet</a> in my room.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-603">
<h3><a name="page-603">Thursday, August 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day had a little <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a><span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Dews</a> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie leaves</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben carried us to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  We helped <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a> <a href='../subjects/7372' title='grape juice'>grape juice</a> and <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7558' title='Jane Wooding'>Mrs Wooding</a> and <a href='../subjects/7375' title='Virginia Smith'>Virginia <span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/7376' title='Virginia Wooding'>Virginia Wooding</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7377' title='Jim Reynolds'>Jim Reynolds</a> to a <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Ben lone him his <span class='line-break'> </span> car.  I hope that nothing <span class='line-break'> </span> wont happen to it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin brought us home this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-604">
<h3><a name="page-604">Friday, August 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> worked in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening we went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  We put up 29 <span class='line-break'> </span> cans.  Ben will stay at <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> come home this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I am glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> have her back.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-605">
<h3><a name="page-605">Saturday, August 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> picked <span class='line-break'> </span> them up.  Ben <a href='../subjects/7378' title='sowing'>sowed</a> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/363' title='seeds'>seed</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a>.  Josie got most <span class='line-break'> </span> of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went after some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> After dinner I put up three <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>cans</a> and killed two <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and cut the <a href='../subjects/7250' title='cucumber'>cucumbers</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> put them in brine.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Paul and <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Dick Woodings</a> to a <a href='../subjects/7380' title='stew'>stew</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  I hope they may have <span class='line-break'> </span> a nice time.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julia</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> are <span class='line-break'> </span> in my room and talk so <span class='line-break'> </span> much that I am in the hall <span class='line-break'> </span> writing.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> cut a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> today.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-606">
<h3><a name="page-606">Sunday, August 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> and <a href='../subjects/7361' title='Julia Brumfield'>Julie</a> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>the Island</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They started home today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I wish they could have staid <span class='line-break'> </span> another week.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home most <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben broke his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am very sorry.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin to <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-607">
<h3><a name="page-607">Monday, August 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this morning.  Clear <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a> this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped this evening as <span class='line-break'> </span> long as we could tie.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> dried out.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Paul went to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a> this evening.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a> wheel broke as they <span class='line-break'> </span> come home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>Pauls tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening for the first time.  <span class='line-break'> </span> It looks good to me.  I am <span class='line-break'> </span> glad of the good crop that is <span class='line-break'> </span> on the place hope it can be <span class='line-break'> </span> taken care of and may do <span class='line-break'> </span> all a lot of good.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-608">
<h3><a name="page-608">Tuesday, August 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canned</a> some <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she scrubbed <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7382' title='kitchen'>cook room</a> floor.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a>.  She is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> but a bout.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I did not see <a href='../subjects/7383' title='Miss Kate'>Miss <span class='line-break'> </span> Kate</a> or <a href='../subjects/7384' title='Mrs Jane'>Mrs Jane</a> they <span class='line-break'> </span> were taking their <a href='../subjects/7385' title='napping'>evening <span class='line-break'> </span> nap</a>.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christine Reynolds</a> and <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> come to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-609">
<h3><a name="page-609">Wednesday, August 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked at home until twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied leaves</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washin <span class='line-break'> </span> of clothes.  This evening <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mag <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> and four of the <span class='line-break'> </span> children come.  I was glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that they did come her baby <span class='line-break'> </span> is just fine.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> the little girls come.  I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad that she could get off.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and the boys <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It was night when they <span class='line-break'> </span> got home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-610">
<h3><a name="page-610">Thursday, August 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> got out <a href='../subjects/7340' title='tobacco sticks'>tobacco sticks</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a> today and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7387' title='damsons'>damsons</a>.  She carried all <span class='line-break'> </span> three of the children with <span class='line-break'> </span> her.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> over here this evening.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> went up to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She was gone to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> and <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Thompson.  We staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while and then <span class='line-break'> </span> went home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Some one <a href='../subjects/7655' title='theft'>stole</a> some of <span class='line-break'> </span> Bens <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> last night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-611">
<h3><a name="page-611">Friday, August 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  They <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> for <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Brand(?) and James(?) <span class='line-break'> </span> Dews</a> helped them.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7387' title='damsons'>damson</a> <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> some.  I <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I was eating <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellon</a> this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> when a <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a> come.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim B</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7389' title='Zack Adkins'>Zack Adkins</a> and <a href='../subjects/7390' title='Smith'>Mr and <span class='line-break'> </span> Mrs Smith</a> was on it.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> come in a few minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Jim Brumfield staid on he is <span class='line-break'> </span> here tonight.  [ink smear] I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> sleep and marked my book.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-612">
<h3><a name="page-612">Saturday, August 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a> a house <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped them finish.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a> come.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad that they did.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and Earl went off <span class='line-break'> </span> some where to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Jim went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-613">
<h3><a name="page-613">Sunday, August 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> some where from here this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley <span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> and two children <span class='line-break'> </span> was here this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben is at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  We heard that <a href='../subjects/7962' title='Joe Edmonds'>Jo<span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a> <a href='../subjects/7392' title='broken bones'>broke his arm</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I am very sorry <span class='line-break'> </span> for him also his folks.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-614">
<h3><a name="page-614">Monday, August 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and a good <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day and is at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> spent the day <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> tobacco nearly all <span class='line-break'> </span> day. <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> tied <span class='line-break'> </span> two.   <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and made <span class='line-break'> </span> a kettle of <a href='../subjects/251' title='preserves'>preserves</a> of <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> that Lizzie <span class='line-break'> </span> brought us.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-615">
<h3><a name="page-615">Tuesday, August 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds a round <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening but no rain here <span class='line-break'> </span> to do any good.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  We all <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> tobacco this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning a while.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped us.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come home <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> and <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>irish potatoes</a> and <a href='../subjects/7394' title='fried apples'>fried <span class='line-break'> </span> apples</a>.  We all enjoyed the <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christine Reynolds</a> come here a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  Heard <span class='line-break'> </span> to day that <a href='../subjects/369' title='Kate Reynolds'>Kate Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/407' title='Clack Hubbard'>Clack Hubbard</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7317' title='wedding'>married</a> yesterday. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Was not surprised much.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> to day.  The first <span class='line-break'> </span> in a long time.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 35 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-616">
<h3><a name="page-616">Wednesday, August 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A day that the men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks could work most of <span class='line-break'> </span> the time.  They moved <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> and scattered <a href='../subjects/7340' title='tobacco sticks'>sticks</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> ready for <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a>.  We all <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a> and finished.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to the <a href='../subjects/7395' title='tomato patch'>tomato patch</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Could not get <span class='line-break'> </span> many <a href='../subjects/250' title='tomatoes'>tomatoes</a>.  Brought a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellon</a> home.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> cut it.  It was fine. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It is raining now <span class='line-break'> </span> hope it may stop soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren <span class='line-break'> </span> Worshams</a> this evening and <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>his mother</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Guess she is at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harveys</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-617">
<h3><a name="page-617">Thursday, August 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Some <a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>clouds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout but no rain to stop work.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> two <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The children and I and <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped what we could.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I think Ben has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>make fires</a> in the <a href='../subjects/7341' title='flues'>flues</a> now.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben has a lot of nice <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a> now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-618">
<h3><a name="page-618">Friday, August 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a> a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house <span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Board? and Tennie? <span class='line-break'> </span> Dews</a> helped them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> come home this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> come this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/348' title='Mrs Edmonds'>Mrs Edmons</a> gave <span class='line-break'> </span> us some <a href='../subjects/7314' title='peaches'>peaches</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We pealed and made <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>pickle</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canned</a> them.  There was <span class='line-break'> </span> enough to do a lot of <span class='line-break'> </span> good.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-619">
<h3><a name="page-619">Saturday, August 31, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Clouds a <span class='line-break'> </span> bout but no rain here to <span class='line-break'> </span> speak of.  The men folks finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting</a> a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> for me.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  She was at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried her <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  Lizzie and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> walked with <span class='line-break'> </span> her some of the way home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> is <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-620">
<h3><a name="page-620">Sunday, September  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  The <span class='line-break'> </span> men folks staid <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>his mother</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> home this morning.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried Josie and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> four of their children.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I spent the day there.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie</a> and <a href='../subjects/409' title='Nannie Reynolds'>Nannie</a> <a href='../subjects/7600' title='Charlotte Reynolds'>and baby</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <a href='../subjects/7653' title='Julia'>Julia</a> and baby.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We had a pleasant day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They had plenty of <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water <span class='line-break'> </span> mellons</a>.  Ben will have <span class='line-break'> </span> to stay at the barns to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 35 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-621">
<h3><a name="page-621">Monday, September  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered tobacco</a>.  Ben and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We had <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> the first peas that <span class='line-break'> </span> we had this year.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blair</a> come over here <span class='line-break'> </span> and got some <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water melons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Paul and Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> will stay <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
