<p> Josie peeled and put out <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> <a href='../subjects/7399' title='drying fruit'>to dry</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-622">
<h3><a name="page-622">Tuesday, September  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> all day and is at the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> now.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7331' title='suckering'>suckered</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> his tobacco this morning.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening he helped <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tie leaves</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening she cut off <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and got two <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-623">
<h3><a name="page-623">Wednesday, September  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barns</a> and <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I washed <span class='line-break'> </span> a little.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> and <a href='../subjects/7333' title='Jane Reynolds'>Jane</a> was here <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I was glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> have them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I wish it would rain <span class='line-break'> </span> we need it so bad.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-624">
<h3><a name="page-624">Thursday, September  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Just at dark <span class='line-break'> </span> it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a>.  It was <span class='line-break'> </span> badly needed.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> got out at three oclock this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> and <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> some this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and [I] helped <span class='line-break'> </span> them some this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We picked some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/7402' title='Lizzie Anderson'>Lizzie <span class='line-break'> </span> Anderson</a> come.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> come.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Virginia wants to learn <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a> and knit a <a href='../subjects/7403' title='sweater'>sweater</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-625">
<h3><a name="page-625">Friday, September  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> some.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I helped <span class='line-break'> </span> to move and Josie helped <span class='line-break'> </span> to unload the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> green tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> a little <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a> come and got <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-626">
<h3><a name="page-626">Saturday, September  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> all day <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> filled four <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>houses</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> and the boys <span class='line-break'> </span> helped them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped to unload <span class='line-break'> </span> every time in the morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She baked three chocolate <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a> for Sundays <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We are looking for <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>Bill Brumfield</a> to morrow. <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope it will not rain so they <span class='line-break'> </span> wont come.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-627">
<h3><a name="page-627">Sunday, September  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>made fires</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> under the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and [I] got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Powers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> brought <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> and <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>Bill</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> to <a href='../subjects/7407' title='Mrs Hendricks'>Mrs Hendricks</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and Josie brought them here.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice Wooding</a> and <a href='../subjects/7298' title='Mrs Winston'>Mrs Winston</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come this evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children come a few minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Dews</a> and <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mayhew</a> and <a href='../subjects/218' title='George Hutcherson'>George <span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> come and played <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>croquet</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-628">
<h3><a name="page-628">Monday, September  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> loaded <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>ready for market</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men will <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>stay at the <span class='line-break'> </span> barn</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped to load <span class='line-break'> </span> the waggon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got most of the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia Fergerson</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> bout sundown.  She got some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> to carry her home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> and <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> come down to <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Paul and <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> up there to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-629">
<h3><a name="page-629">Tuesday, September 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired tobacco</a> all day to day <span class='line-break'> </span> and will stay <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.   <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> carried <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>sold well</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I picked a few <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> and <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie Blair</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> a little while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I did not see them.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> was at the <a href='../subjects/7339' title='bean patch'>bean patch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-632">
<h3><a name="page-632">Friday, September 11, 1918 (revised)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> has taken the day easy.  They killed <span class='line-break'> </span> three <a href='../subjects/7235' title='squirrels'>squirrels</a> this morning.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening Paul carried <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  We come back <span class='line-break'> </span> by <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a>.  Paul <a href='../subjects/7409' title='draft'>registered</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed.  I got a snack <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I stopped a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes at <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.  She looks <span class='line-break'> </span> tired and bad.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Paul are loading the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> with <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-630">
<h3><a name="page-630">Wednesday, September 11, 1918 (original)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a><span class='line-break'> </span> loaded the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> this<span class='line-break'> </span> morning <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>ready for market</a> in<span class='line-break'> </span> the morning.  The men will<span class='line-break'> </span> stay <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> to night<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped to load<span class='line-break'> </span> the waggon.  I got most of<span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We looked for<span class='line-break'> </span> [ink stain] <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia</a> all the<span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They did not come.<span class='line-break'> </span> Julia come a bout sundown.<span class='line-break'> </span> She got a few <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> and some<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/223' title='butter'>butter</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried her<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  To night <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> +<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl</a> come to<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7408' title='Johnsons'>Johnsons</a>.  Paul carried<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> and I up there.  We<span class='line-break'> </span> staid until ten oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> have just got home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> [scratched out]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-631">
<h3><a name="page-631">Thursday, September 12, 1918 (revised)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary</a> and <a href='../subjects/7410' title='William Brumfield, Jr.'>William Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7203' title='Long Island, Virginia'>Long Island</a> to day <span class='line-break'> </span> on their way home.  I do <span class='line-break'> </span> hope they are at <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Mr <a href='../subjects/7411' title='Will Motley'>Will Motley</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening.  He <span class='line-break'> </span> was an <a href='../subjects/7362' title='Odd Fellows'>odd Fellow</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> to <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>a show</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> kept the children.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben and Josie and<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> have gone to see the <span class='line-break'> </span> show.  I am here with the <span class='line-break'> </span> children.  Hope they will <span class='line-break'> </span> be pleased with it.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-634">
<h3><a name="page-634">Saturday, September 12, 1918 (original)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired tobacco</a> all day<span class='line-break'> </span> and will stay at it all night.<span class='line-break'> </span> Paul has got to haul a load<span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  They <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> made a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> to day<span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She went<span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a few minutes<span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I picked a few<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> and <a href='../subjects/206' title='Nettie Blair'>Nettie Blair</a> come<span class='line-break'> </span> over here this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I did not see them.  I was<span class='line-break'> </span> at the <a href='../subjects/7339' title='bean patch'>bean patch</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-633">
<h3><a name="page-633">Friday, September 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> and <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I helped to unload the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben had <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> <a href='../subjects/7413' title='Grey'>Grey</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7414' title='Jake'>Jake</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> had <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7415' title='Pomp'>Pomp</a>.  Carried some <a href='../subjects/7347' title='primings'>primings</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  He went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> on <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blairs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all the <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> to day but <span class='line-break'> </span> did not get his grinding.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Will have to go a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-635">
<h3><a name="page-635">Saturday, September 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> finished moving a <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>house</a> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and filled it with green <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and stayed with the <span class='line-break'> </span> children while <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> before they <span class='line-break'> </span> come home.  Josie and her <span class='line-break'> </span> children.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> at home <span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> has gone home this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> is to come back to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope nothing will happen to <span class='line-break'> </span> him or the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evelyn</a> to day. I was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad to hear from them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-636">
<h3><a name="page-636">Sunday, September 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbards</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/391' title='Sunday School'>Sunday School</a>.  He eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  Paul and <a href='../subjects/301' title='Frank Blair'>Frank <span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> went some where on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>Georges</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  George and <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvins this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> and family <span class='line-break'> </span> was at Marvins.  <a href='../subjects/7268' title='Nat Wooding'>Nat Wooding</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and family and <a href='../subjects/336' title='Alice Wooding'>Miss Alice <span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding</a> was there two.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid at home til three <span class='line-break'> </span> oclock then I went to Marvins.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I had <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bakers bread</a> and <a href='../subjects/7433' title='cheese'>cheese</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for dinner.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> sent them <span class='line-break'> </span> to me.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-637">
<h3><a name="page-637">Monday, September 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7400' title='moving tobacco'>moved</a> two curings of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> and <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> two <a href='../subjects/7434' title='room (barns)'>rooms</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> of green tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> picked up some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> and picked <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> this morning.  In <span class='line-break'> </span> the evening I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes and picked a<span class='line-break'> </span> few more beans then went to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7337' title='tobacco ground'>tobacco ground</a> and helped <span class='line-break'> </span> to load the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> and to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> and helped to unload so <span class='line-break'> </span> as to hurry <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a>.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> wanted to go to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> did not want them to be late.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie had <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> ready when we <span class='line-break'> </span> got to the house.  While we were <span class='line-break'> </span> eating, <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> come and brought <span class='line-break'> </span> me a pan of <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>light bread</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I certainly was glad of the <span class='line-break'> </span> bread.   Was sorry that Denia <span class='line-break'> </span> had so much trouble but I do <span class='line-break'> </span> appreciate it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Paul and Josie are at Altavista tonight.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-638">
<h3><a name="page-638">Tuesday, September 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Just at night <span class='line-break'> </span> we had <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> cloud and <span class='line-break'> </span> a little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut tobacco</a>.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> the boys helped them this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> carried <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladys Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I to <a href='../subjects/7435' title='Jesse Worsham'>Mr Jessie Worshams</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7436' title='mill pond'>mill pond</a>.  I caught one <span class='line-break'> </span> nice <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  We had it cooked<span class='line-break'> </span> it for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> will stay <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>at the barns</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-639">
<h3><a name="page-639">Wednesday, September 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/187' title='cloudy'>Cloudy</a> this morning and some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  The folks finished <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cutting <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped to load and unload <span class='line-break'> </span> the last load.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I both got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went a way from <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.  Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> him.  Josie went two.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was here a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> had a <a href='../subjects/7437' title='farm sale'>sale</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  Solde every thing that he <span class='line-break'> </span> had.  Ben did not go he was <span class='line-break'> </span> so busy with his tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie has not come <span class='line-break'> </span> home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8:40 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-640">
<h3><a name="page-640">Thursday, September 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Had a <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>shower</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout dark.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was afraid <span class='line-break'> </span> that we would have a <a href='../subjects/82' title='storm'>storm</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and come down here with all <span class='line-break'> </span> the little children.  It did not <span class='line-break'> </span> rain long so <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and Carrie and Vera went home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> staid all night. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> to see a show <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Josie and I washed <span class='line-break'> </span> a big washing this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>ried <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and I to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> to <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben and Josie and Henry <span class='line-break'> </span> and Owen and Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> are all gone to Altavista <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/7412' title='a show'>a show</a>.  Hope they <span class='line-break'> </span> may enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-641">
<h3><a name="page-641">Friday, September 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired tobacco</a> all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> had a <a href='../subjects/7438' title='backache'>hurting in her <span class='line-break'> </span> back</a> and was not able to work <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Was some better off <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening and made some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7439' title='sweetmeats'>sweetmeats</a> and <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>pickle</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and then went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am so sorry for Ben tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> It is raining so hard and <span class='line-break'> </span> he is at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-642">
<h3><a name="page-642">Saturday, September 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>fired tobacco</a> all day and will <span class='line-break'> </span> stay with it tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight to the Lodge.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a>.  She was washing <span class='line-break'> </span> her floors up stairs.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> staid <span class='line-break'> </span> with the little children <span class='line-break'> </span> while she was gone.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried Kate home and <span class='line-break'> </span> I come with him back.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> was glad of the ride.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-643">
<h3><a name="page-643">Sunday, September 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  There was some <span class='line-break'> </span> frost this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished <a href='../subjects/7393' title='firing'>firing</a> his <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Ben and family <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Powers</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They were all gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> to <a href='../subjects/7228' title='preaching'>preaching</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They had a good <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I enjoyed it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and the <span class='line-break'> </span> three little children come <span class='line-break'> </span> over there.  I come with them <span class='line-break'> </span> back on the <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and Ben was at <span class='line-break'> </span> home when I got here.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight Marvin and <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William <span class='line-break'> </span> Gilbert</a> are here filling <span class='line-break'> </span> out Williams <a href='../subjects/7409' title='draft'>questionaire</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope he may never <span class='line-break'> </span> have to go to the <a href='../subjects/7567' title='World War I'>war</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-644">
<h3><a name="page-644">Monday, September 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I come with <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George <span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a> folks to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and to <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher Craddocks</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Found them all well.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/301' title='Frank Blair'>Frank Blair</a> a greed <span class='line-break'> </span> to go to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> Chatham.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-645">
<h3><a name="page-645">Tuesday, September 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I spent the day <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7441' title='Joseph Terry Towler'>Jo Towlers</a>.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> were all well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We tried to come by <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7442' title='Craddock cemetery'>grave yard</a>.  I had <span class='line-break'> </span> for got where it was <span class='line-break'> </span> so we did not find it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Got back to <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letchers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> alright.  All well to<span class='line-break'> </span> night at Letchers.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Would like to know how <span class='line-break'> </span> all was at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Do hope they are all well.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-646">
<h3><a name="page-646">Wednesday, September 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/7443' title='Billie Bennett'>Billie <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennetts</a>.  Found them well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7656' title='Paul'>Paul</a> was at Billies.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He gave me his picture.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7444' title='Nannie Bennett'>Nanie</a> had a good <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and some fine <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7324' title='watermelons'>water mellons</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Back at <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letchers</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-647">
<h3><a name="page-647">Thursday, September 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good morning. <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rain</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and I staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letchers</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then <span class='line-break'> </span> went to see <a href='../subjects/7445' title='John Craddock'>John Craddocks <span class='line-break'> </span> sister</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7446' title='Mary Christine Craddock Towler'>Mary Towler</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  Found them well. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> While we were there it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> When we started home <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/357' title='creek'>creek</a> <a href='../subjects/7447' title='flooding'>was up</a> so that we <span class='line-break'> </span> could not cross<span class='line-break'> </span> where we did when we went <span class='line-break'> </span> over there so we crossed <span class='line-break'> </span> on a <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> and crossed two <span class='line-break'> </span> branches on poles and <span class='line-break'> </span> rails.  None of us <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fell</a> or got <span class='line-break'> </span> wet.  We come by the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7442' title='Craddock cemetery'>grave yard</a> and got to <span class='line-break'> </span> Letchers OK.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-648">
<h3><a name="page-648">Friday, September 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We are <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letchers</a>.  We eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> here and then went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7448' title='Elender Bennett'>Elender Bennett</a> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola <span class='line-break'> </span> Jefferson</a>.  I gathered some <span class='line-break'> </span> apple blossoms this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The men here <a href='../subjects/7388' title='tobacco cutting'>cut</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> to night.  They are <span class='line-break'> </span> getting some <a href='../subjects/7449' title='honey'>honey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> ready for me to take home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Letcher has bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-649">
<h3><a name="page-649">Saturday, September 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> was at <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher Craddocks</a>.  Ella <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come for us.  We come by <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  Otho brought me home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> is here tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob</a> and <a href='../subjects/7452' title='Ella Hubbard'>Ella Hubbard</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> all the children come to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7453' title='Sam Hubbard'>Mr Sam Hubbard</a> brough <span class='line-break'> </span> them.  They had bin to <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 12 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-650">
<h3><a name="page-650">Sunday, September 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/7276' title='Robert Hubbard'>Rob Hubbard</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and family spent the day <span class='line-break'> </span> here.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried them <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went with them.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George</a> and <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7450' title='Otho Blair'>Otho</a> and <a href='../subjects/393' title='Sallie Blair'>Sallie Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come here.  <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie Bennett</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went with them home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children and I eat <span class='line-break'> </span> our <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> have all gone to bed.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie have not come <span class='line-break'> </span> home yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-651">
<h3><a name="page-651">Monday, September 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all hands <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobaccco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come home at twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> and fixed a snack to eat.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come but I <span class='line-break'> </span> did not see her.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel Smith</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  I hope she will soon <span class='line-break'> </span> be well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7455' title='Miss Bobsman'>Miss <span class='line-break'> </span> Bobsman</a> wanting to board <span class='line-break'> </span> with me while she teaches <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  Guess she will as <span class='line-break'> </span> no one else will take her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-652">
<h3><a name="page-652">Tuesday, October  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> half of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> put new <span class='line-break'> </span> straw in some of the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7456' title='bed ticks'>bed ticks</a> and picked some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7457' title='pears'>pears</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George <span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs</a> found all of the <span class='line-break'> </span> girls <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> not in bed <span class='line-break'> </span> but should have bin.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7458' title='Mrs Anderson'>Mrs Anderson</a> and <a href='../subjects/230' title='Lizzie Bennett'>Lizzie</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mrs Anderson commenced <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7403' title='sweater'>sweater</a> for her boy <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7459' title='Asa Anderson'>Asa</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip tobacco</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-653">
<h3><a name="page-653">Wednesday, October  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7461' title='Worsham&apos;s pond'>Worshams <span class='line-break'> </span> pond</a> to <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  We did not <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch anything</a> but minnows.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We walked from the <span class='line-break'> </span> pond to the <a href='../subjects/7460' title='union mens lodge'>union mens lodge</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  Ben met us.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> come by <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the children was <span class='line-break'> </span> with Ben.  Nearly all the <span class='line-break'> </span> Blairs are <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel <span class='line-break'> </span> Smith</a> is yet sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I left this book at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7440' title='Letcher Craddock'>Letcher Craddocks</a> got it home <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-654">
<h3><a name="page-654">Thursday, October  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/446' title='South Boston'>South Boston</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Carried <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> on <span class='line-break'> </span> their <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>cars</a>.  They had some <span class='line-break'> </span> trouble but got there in <span class='line-break'> </span> time to <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>sell</a>.  They were very <span class='line-break'> </span> well pleased with the sales. <span class='line-break'> </span> Got home a good while before <span class='line-break'> </span> night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washing <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  To night <span class='line-break'> </span> she has sick <a href='../subjects/375' title='headache'>headache</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I commenced a <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>sock</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> to send to Charlie <span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  There is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> nearly every where at this <span class='line-break'> </span> time.  I do hope that the <span class='line-break'> </span> people may soon get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-655">
<h3><a name="page-655">Friday, October  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut corn</a> and the children <span class='line-break'> </span> helped some.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> me.  We drove <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a>.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> caught several <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  Stopped <span class='line-break'> </span> at Mount Airy a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> thinks I am awful <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout going <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I know it is foolish but I cant <span class='line-break'> </span> help but want to go.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I try to pay for all my <span class='line-break'> </span> trouble.  I work all I am <span class='line-break'> </span> able and not all for my <span class='line-break'> </span> self.  I try to not <span class='line-break'> </span> disgrace them in any way <span class='line-break'> </span> but I know that some <span class='line-break'> </span> of the children are <span class='line-break'> </span> ashamed of me.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-656">
<h3><a name="page-656">Saturday, October  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and wife went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> meet the teacher.  She did not <span class='line-break'> </span> come.  Ben said that he saw <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Tenia Brumfield</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> see <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucuis Gravley</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7464' title='Mrs Dalton'>Mrs Daulton</a> come here <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and got some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> to <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to see <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> while this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-657">
<h3><a name="page-657">Sunday, October  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  A little <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> not enought to do any harm.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while this evening.  I did <span class='line-break'> </span> not go.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> and Christine <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> come a little while.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The meeting starts at <a href='../subjects/7465' title='St Andrews'>St Andrews</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-658">
<h3><a name="page-658">Monday, October  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men <span class='line-break'> </span> folks <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut corn</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> mowed <a href='../subjects/355' title='peas'>peas</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The rest of them cut corn <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Little Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> boys worked at it all <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening we <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7466' title='picking peas'>picked peas</a>.  <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice</a> picked all the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7468' title='Mrs Dawson'>Mrs Dawson</a> come after some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> and got them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> cooked the first <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> on her new range this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Tobacco was so dry that we <span class='line-break'> </span> could not strip this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We had <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> and <a href='../subjects/7330' title='cornbread'>cornbread</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-659">
<h3><a name="page-659">Tuesday, October  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> the children <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cut corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William <span class='line-break'> </span> Gilbert</a> helped half of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> see a bout some <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> that he bought from <a href='../subjects/7470' title='Mrs Berger'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Berger</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and <a href='../subjects/7466' title='picking peas'>picked peas</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I picked some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> was <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>canning</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-660">
<h3><a name="page-660">Wednesday, October  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day there was frost <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  The men finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7469' title='cutting corn'>cutting corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/7471' title='Luke'>Luke</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> finished the corn while the others <span class='line-break'> </span> shocked.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I picked a few <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/7472' title='sulphering apples'>sulphered</a> some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and made some <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>pickle</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I dug a few <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> cut the <a href='../subjects/7256' title='sunflowers'>sun flowers</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> To night <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/364' title='plow points'>plow points</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-661">
<h3><a name="page-661">Thursday, October 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/325' title='Paul Smith'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a> and <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come down here a little while <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I tried to <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> this evening.  It got so dry <span class='line-break'> </span> that we could not tie it as <span class='line-break'> </span> it should be done.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a little while late <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She wanted to <span class='line-break'> </span> see Ben.  We walked over <span class='line-break'> </span> where he was <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowing</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have just finished stringing <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-662">
<h3><a name="page-662">Friday, October 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> this morning.  This <span class='line-break'> </span> evening <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> raked pea <span class='line-break'> </span> vines.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped a little <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  We got our <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning before we went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> cooked <a href='../subjects/7277' title='green beans'>snaps</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7474' title='baking bread'>baked bread</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Come home at twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> and made <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> In the evening the tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> dried out so we could not <span class='line-break'> </span> tie it.  I picked up some <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and gathered some snaps.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> and strung <span class='line-break'> </span> our snaps.  Come home.  Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> the <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I fed the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We had to <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shuck the corn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has just got back <span class='line-break'> </span> from Bailiss and eat his <span class='line-break'> </span> supper.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-663">
<h3><a name="page-663">Saturday, October 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Cloudy today and some <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> got up part of his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7475' title='pea hay'>pea hay</a> and part got wet.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> when we got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> thought we would <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip tobacco</a>.  It was so dry <span class='line-break'> </span> that we could not handle <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I dug some <a href='../subjects/239' title='potatoes'>potatoes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> helped me and <span class='line-break'> </span> we built a <a href='../subjects/7227' title='pigpen'>pig pen</a> and got up <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> and they got out.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> went a <a href='../subjects/7476' title='squirrel hunting'>squirrel <span class='line-break'> </span> hunting</a>.  Killed four.  Ben kept <span class='line-break'> </span> 2 and then would not <span class='line-break'> </span> skin them.  So I did it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and <a href='../subjects/7260' title='Lonnie Bennett'>Lonnie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> are <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  Had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a>.  They were <span class='line-break'> </span> well when she <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope that they may stay so.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-664">
<h3><a name="page-664">Sunday, October 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  we all stayed <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7379' title='turnips'>turnip salit</a> and <a href='../subjects/7237' title='butter beans'>butter beans</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> helped <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> move <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> while it was in <span class='line-break'> </span> order.  This evening <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> family and <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin <span class='line-break'> </span> Harvey</a> come.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and some of the children <span class='line-break'> </span> was here and <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>played croquet</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/231' title='Earl Bennett'>Earl Bennett</a> come.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul will stay a while and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip tobacco</a>.  I hope that <span class='line-break'> </span> it may stay in order so he <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7371' title='canning'>can</a> handle it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-665">
<h3><a name="page-665">Monday, October 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> hauled <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7475' title='pea hay'>pea hay</a> this morning and <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Little Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/416' title='Beatrice Owen'>Beatrice Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> come and got some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> and brough us some <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and carried 4 <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chickens</a> and 2 doz <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>.  Bough <a href='../subjects/7477' title='soap'>soap</a> and <a href='../subjects/113' title='oil'>oil</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben and Paul and Owen <span class='line-break'> </span> are at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> putting tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-666">
<h3><a name="page-666">Tuesday, October 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>and I <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>worked on tobacco</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span>morning.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span>on the <a href='../subjects/7478' title='wheat land'>wheat land</a>.</p>
<p>Rev. Paget and  East come this <span class='line-break'> </span>evening selling Liberty Bonds.  <span class='line-break'> </span>I let them have nearly all <span class='line-break'> </span>the money I had.
