I did <span class='line-break'> </span>not want to do it but did <span class='line-break'> </span>not know what to do.</p>
<p>Ben and Josie and Franklin <span class='line-break'> </span>went to |Jim Powers] this             or is this Towers?<span class='line-break'> </span>evening.  Ben bought <span class='line-break'> </span>some oats from Power and <span class='line-break'> </span>some wheat from <a href='../subjects/7483' title='J Starkey'>Jr <span class='line-break'> </span>Starkey</a>.  Jim Power come <span class='line-break'> </span>up here this evening eat <span class='line-break'> </span>supper here.  He got some <span class='line-break'> </span>rye</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-667">
<h3><a name="page-667">Wednesday, October 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed <span class='line-break'> </span> wheat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  Heard today <span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/7485' title='John McCormick'>John McCormic</a> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  I never have heard <span class='line-break'> </span> of as many deaths and as <span class='line-break'> </span> much <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> as there is now.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The <a href='../subjects/7486' title='warehouses'>ware houses</a> has closed for <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce Reynolds</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> home yester day.  <a href='../subjects/7487' title='Mrs Cook'>Mrs Cook</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnsons</a> visiting.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7488' title='Mrs Starkey'>Mrs Starkeys</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/7489' title='seed wheat'>seed wheat</a>.  He went on <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-668">
<h3><a name="page-668">Thursday, October 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> today.  The rest of us <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> come home and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> boys was <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening and had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> with them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> fixed him a <a href='../subjects/7490' title='dumb bull'>dumb <span class='line-break'> </span> bull</a> today.  He thinks it <span class='line-break'> </span> great.  To night Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for some thing to eat.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There is lots of <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a round.  Ben had a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> today <span class='line-break'> </span> he was well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-669">
<h3><a name="page-669">Friday, October 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> sowed<span class='line-break'> </span>oats and some wheat.</p>
<p>The rest of us stripped <span class='line-break'> </span>tobacco.  Ben <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span>hauled some and put it in <span class='line-break'> </span>the pit.  It was so dark they <span class='line-break'> </span>had the lanterns to work by.</p>
<p>We heard today that <span class='line-break'> </span>[Chesley Edmons] and [Lucius Gravely]  {Ga---ly?}<span class='line-break'> </span>got a call to go tocamp.</p>
<p>Oh this awful time when will <span class='line-break'> </span>it be any better no one knows.</p>
<p>10 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-670">
<h3><a name="page-670">Saturday, October 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/274' title='cool'>cool</a> and <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  Come home <span class='line-break'> </span> and hauled a load of <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> at <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> did not get his grinding.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7494' title='Posie Johnson'>Posie Johnson</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> heard this evening that <a href='../subjects/376' title='Posey Reynolds'>Posie <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> is sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished digging the <a href='../subjects/7264' title='sweet potatoes'>sweet <span class='line-break'> </span> potatoes</a> and Paul hauled <span class='line-break'> </span> them home on the <a href='../subjects/7495' title='wheel barrow'>wheel <span class='line-break'> </span> barrow</a>.  <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come by here this evening <span class='line-break'> </span> to tell us good by he has <span class='line-break'> </span> got to go to <a href='../subjects/7496' title='training camp'>training camp</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Monday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-671">
<h3><a name="page-671">Sunday, October 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We all stayed <span class='line-break'> </span> at home until late in the <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a while.  I walked with <span class='line-break'> </span> Kate as far as <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There has bin very little passing <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-672">
<h3><a name="page-672">Monday, October 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> with <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a> <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius <span class='line-break'> </span> Gravley</a> and <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7352' title='Faber Jefferson'>Faber Jefferson</a> and lots of others <span class='line-break'> </span> had to start to <a href='../subjects/7496' title='training camp'>training camp</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutcherson</a> <a href='../subjects/7505' title='disking'>disked</a> Bens <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> land this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> for one dollar per acre.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We that was <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/7471' title='Luke'>Luke</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7506' title='Norman Owen'>Norman Owen</a> all <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco</a>.  To night Ben and Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to <a href='../subjects/7507' title='rebulking'>rebulk</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie gave me a nice lot of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> a present from Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.  Tomorrow is my <span class='line-break'> </span> birthday.  I will be 72 <span class='line-break'> </span> years olde.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I thank them both.  Mother.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-673">
<h3><a name="page-673">Tuesday, October 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I and the children finished <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping</a> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Pauls</a> <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>curing</a> of tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and commenced on <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a>s.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie come home to get <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She fried <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and baked <a href='../subjects/169' title='coconut'>cocoanut</a> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.  A bout <span class='line-break'> </span> twelve <a href='../subjects/273' title='Gordon Bennett'>Gordon</a> and <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma</a> and <a href='../subjects/428' title='Ola Bennett Jefferson'>Ola</a> and <a href='../subjects/7508' title='Frances Bennett'>Frances <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> come for dinner.  After dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/406' title='Bruce Reynolds'>Bruce Reynolds</a> and <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>his mother</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes.  I was glad to see them <span class='line-break'> </span> all.  Ben <a href='../subjects/7484' title='sowing wheat'>sowed</a> wheat most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  This evening <a href='../subjects/7268' title='Nat Wooding'>Nat Wooding</a> <a href='../subjects/158' title='telephones'>phoned</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for Ben to come to Reynolds mail <span class='line-break'> </span> box and help him work on his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben went.  They could not fix it.  They <span class='line-break'> </span> brought it here.  <a href='../subjects/7510' title='Sidney Reynolds'>Sidney Reynolds</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> after Nat and carried him home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Paul finished sowing wheat.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> gave me a nice box of <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> a birth day <span class='line-break'> </span> present.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin Smith</a> paid our taxes <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  Paul and Ben has <span class='line-break'> </span> bin at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to night hangin <span class='line-break'> </span> and putting tobacco in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-674">
<h3><a name="page-674">Wednesday, October 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  There was a <a href='../subjects/7543' title='killing frost'>killing <span class='line-break'> </span> frost</a> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/7268' title='Nat Wooding'>Nat Woodings</a> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>car</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Nat come tonight and got <span class='line-break'> </span> his car.  Ben went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this evening to see <span class='line-break'> </span> about getting some <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The rest of us and Owen and <span class='line-break'> </span> two of his children helped <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They put some tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> and got a few <a href='../subjects/7398' title='apples'>apples</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-675">
<h3><a name="page-675">Thursday, October 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all except <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> until <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben <a href='../subjects/165' title='horseshoes'>shod</a> the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening he went to Level <span class='line-break'> </span> Run after <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> and carried <span class='line-break'> </span> it to <a href='../subjects/7511' title='Willie Hubbard'>Willie Hubbards</a> <a href='../subjects/7512' title='planer'>planer</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Never got home til after dark.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> gathered up the <a href='../subjects/7226' title='peanuts'>peanuts</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and washed them.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> made a nice lot of them.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I finished the <a href='../subjects/333' title='socks'>socks</a> that I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a> for <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charley Harvey</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a> come for them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-676">
<h3><a name="page-676">Friday, October 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and a little <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on his <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  This evening he <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7522' title='Level Run, Virginia'>Level Run</a> for a load <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> <a href='../subjects/283' title='plowing'>plowed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and fixed rows for <a href='../subjects/312' title='strawberries'>straw berries</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span>  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> the vines.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and his crowd <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a>.  I helped a <span class='line-break'> </span> little before <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie got dinner.  She had to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut</a> her <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> to cook with.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening Josie and I both <span class='line-break'> </span> helped on the tobacco.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We are out of <a href='../subjects/7523' title='flour'>flour</a>.  Ben has <span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/7293' title='Mr Thompson'>Thompsons</a> to night to <span class='line-break'> </span> get some.  We have <a href='../subjects/7263' title='wheat'>wheat</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> but the miller is <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a> enough to grind it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> has caught two <a href='../subjects/7312' title='rabbits'>rabbits</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in his traps.  He is very proud <span class='line-break'> </span> of that.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-677">
<h3><a name="page-677">Saturday, October 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> hauled some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>stalks</a> and put them on the <a href='../subjects/7478' title='wheat land'>wheat land</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  All the rest of us <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  This evening <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/44' title='mill'>mill</a> for <a href='../subjects/7523' title='flour'>flour</a>.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> had <a href='../subjects/7525' title='corn bread'>corn bread</a> for <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I know we should be thankful <span class='line-break'> </span> for that but we have not bin used to <span class='line-break'> </span> it and do not like it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We tied all the tobacco that was in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> then I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went <a href='../subjects/7476' title='squirrel hunting'>squirrel hunting</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They killed nine <a href='../subjects/7235' title='squirrels'>squirrels</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben has gone with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-678">
<h3><a name="page-678">Sunday, October 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day and very <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> for the <span class='line-break'> </span> time of the year.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We all staid at home til <span class='line-break'> </span> twelve.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went a way <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening I don't know <span class='line-break'> </span> where.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the <span class='line-break'> </span> children went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There has bin very little <span class='line-break'> </span> passing here today.  There is <span class='line-break'> </span> so much <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> and <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>death</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the country I think <span class='line-break'> </span> every one ought to stay at <span class='line-break'> </span> home all that they can.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7526' title='William Baily'>William Baily</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> today.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-679">
<h3><a name="page-679">Monday, October 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day no rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and I went by <a href='../subjects/971' title='Java, Virginia'>Java</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and on to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  Kate put in <span class='line-break'> </span> a plea for <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley Edmons</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> come home and strip his <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> for me <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and the <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> and Josie helped <span class='line-break'> </span> what she could.  Ben and I got <span class='line-break'> </span> back a bout <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> time.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Eat dinner.  Ben went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> got done be fore night.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> is very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> hope <span class='line-break'> </span> he may be better soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Had a Letter from <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that he was well.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope he may stay well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-680">
<h3><a name="page-680">Tuesday, October 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and a little <span class='line-break'> </span> rain here.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> just got in <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  Says that it <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rained</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hard there.  He went for a load <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.  The rest of us <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all day.  We <span class='line-break'> </span> finished a <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>curing</a> for <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and commenced one for <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> <a href='../subjects/7392' title='broken bones'>broke her arm</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> yesterday.  I am so sorry for her <span class='line-break'> </span> and her mother.  Would go to see <span class='line-break'> </span> her if it wont for there is <span class='line-break'> </span> so much <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> a bout.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/7527' title='Charles Rorer'>Mr Charles <span class='line-break'> </span> Rorrer</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> to day. <span class='line-break'> </span> He was a soldier in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7528' title='Civil War'>Civil War</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7529' title='Carlton Trent'>Carlton Trent</a> carried <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a> yesterday and to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-681">
<h3><a name="page-681">Wednesday, October 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and the <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>wind</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> blowin to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed logs</a> to carry to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a>.  The rest of us <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7532' title='Lowell Witcher'>Mr Lowel Witcher</a> come and <span class='line-break'> </span> eat dinner with us.  <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come and looked at the <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and Owen <span class='line-break'> </span> put tobacco in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry is <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> of a sore <span class='line-break'> </span> throat to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> It is <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>raining</a> to night hope <span class='line-break'> </span> it will quit soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben put <a href='../subjects/165' title='horseshoes'>shoes</a> on <a href='../subjects/112' title='Dodson Bailiss'>Mr Bailiss's</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horse</a> to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-682">
<h3><a name="page-682">Thursday, October 31, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> got <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> and <a href='../subjects/7533' title='hauling logs'>hauled logs</a> and worked four <span class='line-break'> </span> horses to the <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a>.  <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> to load on the logs.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Paul carried <a href='../subjects/150' title='Dr. Anderson Owen'>Dr Owen</a> to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> this morning.  He had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>Bens car</a>.  <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span> a very <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> childe the Dr was <span class='line-break'> </span> to see it today.  <a href='../subjects/228' title='Clifton Reynolds'>Clifton</a> is still <span class='line-break'> </span> very sick.  Marvin and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I and the <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen children and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> finished <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripping</a> a <a href='../subjects/7354' title='curing'>curing</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> of tobacco for Paul.  We finished a<span class='line-break'> </span> bout twelve.  This evening<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/7534' title='Dorothea Worsham'>Doratha Worsham</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7535' title='Ada Hutcherson'>Ada Hutcherson</a> come a while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7284' title='Ellen Bailiss'>Ellen Bailiss</a> and <a href='../subjects/7536' title='Louise Hutcherson'>Louise Hutcherson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to bring some <span class='line-break'> </span> patterns that Josie let <a href='../subjects/7943' title='Mamie Hutcherson'>Mamie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> have.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-683">
<h3><a name="page-683">Friday, November  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/7533' title='hauling logs'>hauled logs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> carried <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> and I to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I caught 4 <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a> and two <a href='../subjects/7282' title='eels'>eels</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I tried to get some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> at <a href='../subjects/7541' title='Mt. Airy, Virginia'>Mt Airy</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Could not get it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben and Owen and <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul went to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> to put <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-684">
<h3><a name="page-684">Saturday, November  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> has <a href='../subjects/7533' title='hauling logs'>hauled logs</a> and <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all day today.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked some corn</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> This evening they put a load <span class='line-break'> </span> of <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> on the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggons</a>.  <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William <span class='line-break'> </span> Gilbert</a> helped them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.  I got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> except making the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a>.  Josie made that.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Late this evening I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  She was <a href='../subjects/309' title='bathing'>bathing</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> the children and <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> of the <a href='../subjects/66' title='toothache'>toothache</a>.  We heard this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening that <a href='../subjects/7542' title='Eugene Shelton'>Mr Eujean Shelton</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> To night Ben and Owen and <span class='line-break'> </span> Paul went to the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to put on a load of <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco.  They intend going to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> Monday.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-685">
<h3><a name="page-685">Sunday, November  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/279' title='beautiful'>beautiful</a> day.  There was <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7543' title='killing frost'>killing frost</a> last night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We all staid at home until <span class='line-break'> </span> after twelve.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr Powers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  All at home a gain <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> want to start to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning at three oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/203' title='Alma Bennett'>Alma Bennett</a> was at Gretna <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  She talked with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> Smith.  I was very glad <span class='line-break'> </span> that she did.  I am always glad <span class='line-break'> </span> to hear from them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-686">
<h3><a name="page-686">Monday, November  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We got up this morning at <span class='line-break'> </span> two oclock.  The men folks <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and they eat and got <span class='line-break'> </span> off to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with two <span class='line-break'> </span> loads of <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a>.  There was <span class='line-break'> </span> so much tobacco at Gretna <span class='line-break'> </span> they could not <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>sell</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> They got home nine oclock <span class='line-break'> </span> at night.  Josie got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> stayed with <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> children <span class='line-break'> </span> while Marvin and Carrie went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  Carrie had some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>work done on her teeth</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I picked some dried <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> To night Josie and I <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> two <a href='../subjects/7252' title='buckets'>buckets</a> full.  Before they <span class='line-break'> </span> were shelled <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a few minutes.  She wanted <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-687">
<h3><a name="page-687">Tuesday, November  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> is one of <span class='line-break'> </span> the Judges at <a href='../subjects/7546' title='election'>Elections</a>.  He was at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> all day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled some wood</a>.  We needed <span class='line-break'> </span> it mighty bad.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese</a> put some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.  Josie staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> her self and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> carried Reese and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> I to <a href='../subjects/7548' title='Banister River'>Banister River</a> to <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fish</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We caught twenty one fish.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> gave us a nice mess of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/466' title='steak'>steak</a> we had it for <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/7549' title='Max Creasy'>Max Creasy</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> this morning.  I am sorry for <span class='line-break'> </span> the family.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have <a href='../subjects/7355' title='shelling'>shelled</a> a few <a href='../subjects/304' title='beans'>beans</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Am most a sleep <span class='line-break'> </span> now.  Heard today that <a href='../subjects/7659' title='Jesse M. Hutcherson'>Jessie <span class='line-break'> </span> Hutcherson</a> is at home on <a href='../subjects/7551' title='furlough'>furlow</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for 48 hours.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-688">
<h3><a name="page-688">Wednesday, November  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde</a> their <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  It solde <span class='line-break'> </span> very well.  They got home a while <span class='line-break'> </span> after twelve eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> then <span class='line-break'> </span> went to the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>saw mill</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> got a load of <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mr Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7864' title='Rena Mayhew'>Rena</a> went with them <span class='line-break'> </span> also <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went up there and kept <span class='line-break'> </span> the children.  They left <a href='../subjects/222' title='Hazel Smith'>Hazel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  Josie says that they <span class='line-break'> </span> done fine.  I went up to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little while then <span class='line-break'> </span> come home.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> come with <span class='line-break'> </span> me.  We <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> corn enough to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> on to night and in the <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  Ben has gone up <span class='line-break'> </span> to Marvins to help hunt a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/339' title='mink'>mink</a> that killed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-689">
<h3><a name="page-689">Thursday, November  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> hauled <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> from the <a href='../subjects/7552' title='saw mill'>mill</a>.  He brough <span class='line-break'> </span> three loads.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> There was no one at home but <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a>.  George had gone to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  The rest of them <span class='line-break'> </span> had gone to <a href='../subjects/7549' title='Max Creasy'>Max Creasys</a> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7553' title='John Dalton'>John Dalton</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  There is more <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>deaths</a> than I ever heard <span class='line-break'> </span> of in the same length of time.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard today that <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Dick Wooding</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> is very sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight Ben and Josie has gone <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> for groceries.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-690">
<h3><a name="page-690">Friday, November  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hauled a load of <a href='../subjects/171' title='lumber'>lumber</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7554' title='Davis&apos;s mill'>Davis's mill</a> this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7280' title='Hubbards'>Hubbards</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed some this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace</a> and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> and I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7206' title='White Falls, Virginia'>White Falls</a> <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>fishing</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> Did not <a href='../subjects/465' title='fish'>catch any</a> thing.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Grace carried me on the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/268' title='buggy'>buggy</a>.  I did not get home <span class='line-break'> </span> until dark.  I <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie washed dishes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben caught a <a href='../subjects/453' title='pig'>pig</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning and broke its leg.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I hope it may get well.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-691">
<h3><a name="page-691">Saturday, November  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> rais a shed <span class='line-break'> </span> for a <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.  I put two panes of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7555' title='glazing'>glass in the window</a> at the pit.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> two shocks of <span class='line-break'> </span> corn.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> She baked <a href='../subjects/7556' title='potato biscuit'>potato biscuit</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> She baked <a href='../subjects/7557' title='corn batter bread'>corn batter bread</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> I did enjoy it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7884' title='Willie Wooding'>Miss Willie Wooding</a> come a while <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Richard</a> and <a href='../subjects/7558' title='Jane Wooding'>Jane <span class='line-break'> </span> Wooding</a> are both <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> has two children sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin loaded his <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> day intends going to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Monday.  <a href='../subjects/269' title='Earnest Craddock'>Earnest</a> and <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Blairs</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worsham</a> and Ben Brumfield <span class='line-break'> </span> has gone to <a href='../subjects/7213' title='Lynchburg, Virginia'>Lynchburg</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Dont know when to look <span class='line-break'> </span> for them back.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie is ironing yet.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 7 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-692">
<h3><a name="page-692">Sunday, November 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  We all staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home until twelve then <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhews</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie straitened up in my <span class='line-break'> </span> room and <a href='../subjects/7560' title='sweeping'>swept the floor</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Something that is not often <span class='line-break'> </span> done.  I was glad that she <span class='line-break'> </span> did it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladys</a> and <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7562' title='Stuart Owen'>Stewart</a> and <a href='../subjects/441' title='Delma Owen'>Delma Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see the children <span class='line-break'> </span> here.  I think they had <span class='line-break'> </span> a good time.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes.  I did not get <span class='line-break'> </span> to speak to him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie dressed a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  She thinks now <span class='line-break'> </span> that they will start to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> in the morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Layne</a> come this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> to get his <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  He couldn't <span class='line-break'> </span> get it to follow him.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-693">
<h3><a name="page-693">Monday, November 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> commenced on a room for <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> store and bough some things <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children started to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/7564' title='Miss Sneed'>Miss Sneed</a> came <span class='line-break'> </span> to day to be [scratched out "principle"]<span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/7565' title='Harmony Grove'>Harmony Grove</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie Gravley</a> stopped in <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie is at the <a href='../subjects/34' title='barn'>barn</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> working on <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> today <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>solde tobacco</a> for a good <span class='line-break'> </span> price.  Ben and Josie and Marvin <span class='line-break'> </span> has just come from the barn.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-694">
<h3><a name="page-694">Tuesday, November 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> except <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  He <span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a>.  I hope that <span class='line-break'> </span> he may get well soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here to day and eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with us.  While she was <span class='line-break'> </span> here we heard that <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley <span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a> was <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>.  We all <span class='line-break'> </span> are so sorry for them <span class='line-break'> </span> all.  The papers tell that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7567' title='World War I'>peace</a> has bin declared.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> do hope that it is true.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Kate got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> both of her boys that is <span class='line-break'> </span> in <a href='../subjects/7568' title='France'>France</a>.  <a href='../subjects/51' title='Jack Harvey'>Jack</a> is in the <span class='line-break'> </span> hospital hope that he may be <span class='line-break'> </span> well soon.  Tonight Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7522' title='Level Run, Virginia'>Level Run</a> guess they will be <span class='line-break'> </span> back soon.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-695">
<h3><a name="page-695">Wednesday, November 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  Ben helped to dig Chesley Edmons grave to day.  Josie has bin sick most of the day.  She has the head ache to night very bad.  Ben and Jim Emerson come here for dinner.  I had not fixed any thought Ben would be at Mr Edmons for dinner.  We soon got them a snack.  Am all ways glad to see Mr Jim.  Mrs Jessie and Mrs George Hutcherson stoped in here a while this evening.  Murptist Harvey commenced on Marvins frame for his pit to day.  Hope he will soon finish it.  Ben has gone to Strait Stone to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span> Little Edna Jenings was buried to day.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-696">
<h3><a name="page-696">Thursday, November 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> got home by <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> time.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> some <a href='../subjects/7569' title='garments'>garments</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  We got a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for dinner.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a>.  She was making a <a href='../subjects/98' title='dress'>dress</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for her self.  They had a <span class='line-break'> </span> mighty <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> <a href='../subjects/453' title='pig'>pig</a>.  I think it <span class='line-break'> </span> will <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>die</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/136' title='John Smith'>Mr</a> and <a href='../subjects/7571' title='Mrs John Smith'>Mrs John Smith</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> to see <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  They had two of the <span class='line-break'> </span> girls with them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owens</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-697">
<h3><a name="page-697">Friday, November 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>house</a> a little while <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a> come and <span class='line-break'> </span> went up on the house and could <span class='line-break'> </span> not find a leak.  He was here <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  We all but <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/105' title='Chesley Edmonds'>Chesley <span class='line-break'> </span> Edmons</a> <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>burial</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a crowd there.  He <span class='line-break'> </span> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> by the odd <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fell</a>ows.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I am very sorry for the family.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Henry and Edna went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Two of the <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>teachers</a> were at <span class='line-break'> </span> the burial.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-700">
<h3><a name="page-700">Monday, November 16, 1918 (original)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Before we finished eating <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Layne</a> come to get his <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got him in the stable and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> tied him but they could not <span class='line-break'> </span> carry him home he was so stubborn.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> lost about two hours <span class='line-break'> </span> time then they went to work.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben put a <a href='../subjects/7572' title='yoke'>yoke</a> in the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cow</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I worked on the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> nearly <span class='line-break'> </span> all the morning.   The <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calves</a> was in <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/321' title='pasture'>pasture</a> to night.  Ben worked on his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>C Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come a while this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/343' title='planting'>planted</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/7575' title='hyacinths'>hyacinths</a> bulbs to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I brought in my <a href='../subjects/7576' title='dahlias'>daghlia <span class='line-break'> </span> roots</a> this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I put on a pair of new <a href='../subjects/7577' title='shoes'>shoes</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I went up [ink mark]<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Well I went to sleep and made a mark.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-698">
<h3><a name="page-698">Saturday, November 16, 1918 (revised)</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Layne</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was here early this morning after<span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> that was here.  They caught<span class='line-break'> </span> it and then could not carrie it<span class='line-break'> </span> home.  It was so sullen they could<span class='line-break'> </span> not make it go.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> lost <span class='line-break'> </span> a bought two hours with it.  Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> put a <a href='../subjects/7572' title='yoke'>yoke</a> on one of the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> here this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christenia <span class='line-break'> </span> Reynolds</a> come a while this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a few minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> has gone to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfields</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a> brough the clothes <span class='line-break'> </span> that <a href='../subjects/73' title='Hattie Gilbert'>Hattie</a> washed after they <span class='line-break'> </span> was gone.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-699">
<h3><a name="page-699">Sunday, November 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We all staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> children all come up here and played <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7229' title='croquet'>croquet</a>.  I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while.  Marvin went to see <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/18' title='Edmonds'>Edmons</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/104' title='Tom Edmonds'>Tom Edmons</a> went back to <a href='../subjects/7496' title='training camp'>camp</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> <a href='../subjects/466' title='steak'>steak</a> for <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia</a> sent the beef to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and she sent us part of it.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We certainly did enjoy it.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 7 : O clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-702">
<h3><a name="page-702">Wednesday, November 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>Mostly <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> today Had a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> <a href='../subjects/82' title='storm'>storm</a> late.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked</a> corn nearly all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen children helped.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie Gravley</a> and <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> are here to night I am glad to <span class='line-break'> </span> have them.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> B <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I am so anxious to <span class='line-break'> </span> hear from <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There is so much <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> I <span class='line-break'> </span> am a fraid he is sick.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I am a shamed to <span class='line-break'> </span> make so many mistakes. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> [This page is pasted over the original entry for November 16, which Julia had accidentally written on the page for November 18.]</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-701">
<h3><a name="page-701">Tuesday, November 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> in the <a href='../subjects/65' title='woods'>woods</a>.  Ben went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone</a> at twelve oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>stripped tobacco</a> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Owen</a> helped us this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come a few minutes this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> gave me some <a href='../subjects/7580' title='raspberry roots'>rasberry <span class='line-break'> </span> briars</a> to day.  I want to plant <span class='line-break'> </span> them in the morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He was well when he <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am in dread most all the time <span class='line-break'> </span> that some of us will have <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/214' title='influenza'>the dreadful disease</a> that is going<span class='line-break'> </span> a round.  There is two <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>died</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day not too far off from here.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-703">
<h3><a name="page-703">Wednesday, November 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> helped us <a href='../subjects/76' title='stripping tobacco'>strip tobacco</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> until twelve.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid with <span class='line-break'> </span> the children while <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a> to have <span class='line-break'> </span> her <a href='../subjects/7545' title='dentistry'>teeth worked on</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/349' title='Minnie Owen'>Mrs Owen</a> and I <a href='../subjects/7357' title='tying'>tied</a> tobacco <span class='line-break'> </span> all the evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> tied some <span class='line-break'> </span> tobacco to night <span class='line-break'> </span> and put some in the <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-704">
<h3><a name="page-704">Thursday, November 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> hauled <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> a little.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  This evening I <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> they <span class='line-break'> </span> were all well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben loaded the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a>.  Owen and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> helped him.  <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> brought a <span class='line-break'> </span> few <a href='../subjects/7340' title='tobacco sticks'>sticks</a> of tobacco to carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> to market.  They put it on the <span class='line-break'> </span> waggon be fore they eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
