<p> Ben got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul <span class='line-break'> </span> Bennett</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> sent a load of wood to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> to day.  <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee B</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> sent one yesterday.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7581' title='Murphist Harvey'>Murphist Harvey</a> finished <span class='line-break'> </span> his work at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-705">
<h3><a name="page-705">Friday, November 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p><a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>Colde</a> and <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a> with a <span class='line-break'> </span> load of <a href='../subjects/128' title='tobacco sale'>tobacco</a> for <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> him self and a little for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a>.  It all sold <span class='line-break'> </span> reasonably well.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening I <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> my <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7403' title='sweater'>sweater</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7583' title='Mrs Gravley'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Gravley</a> come in a few minutes <span class='line-break'> </span> on their way from <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7563' title='Mr Layne'>Mr Layne</a> come this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> to try to get his <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  He could not <span class='line-break'> </span> manage him and he is here <span class='line-break'> </span> yet.  Ben got home from Gretna <span class='line-break'> </span> about sundown.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I watered and <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> of the <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> be fore he got <span class='line-break'> </span> home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-706">
<h3><a name="page-706">Saturday, November 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7547' title='hauling wood'>hauled wood</a> this morning and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> it this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/182' title='mending'>mended</a> her <a href='../subjects/84' title='fireplace'>fire place</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> cooked <a href='../subjects/7584' title='salsify'>salsify</a> and <a href='../subjects/7585' title='parsnips'>parsnips</a> the <span class='line-break'> </span> [first] that we have had this season.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>worked some button <span class='line-break'> </span> holes</a> in the childrens clothes.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Tonight I have ripped up an old <span class='line-break'> </span> skirt of <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> that <a href='../subjects/7885' title='Alice Hubbard'>Miss <span class='line-break'> </span> Alice Hubbard</a> made before <span class='line-break'> </span> Carrie was married.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> She is thinking of making some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/90' title='pants'>pants</a> for <a href='../subjects/212' title='Roy Smith'>Roy</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben has gone to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/85' title='lodge'>lodge</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-707">
<h3><a name="page-707">Sunday, November 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day very <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim Powers</a>. <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> came <span class='line-break'> </span> with them home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children and I staid at <span class='line-break'> </span> home.  No one came to see us.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> is hoarse to night <span class='line-break'> </span> but hope that he will soon <span class='line-break'> </span> be better of his <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> come down to see <span class='line-break'> </span> a bout putting <a href='../subjects/454' title='tobacco'>tobacco</a> in the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.  They did not put any in.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-708">
<h3><a name="page-708">Monday, November 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7587' title='cattle killing'>killed</a> a <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> helped him.  They both <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/162' title='wood cutting'>cut wood</a> at <a href='../subjects/335' title='Margaret Brumfield'>Mags</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed some this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I stewed <a href='../subjects/7251' title='pumpkin'>pumpkins</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I did not stay but a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie Gravley</a> and <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come here to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Mr Owen and <a href='../subjects/7471' title='Luke'>Luke</a> come in a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes.  Mr Owen played <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7588' title='fiddle'>fiddle</a> a little while.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Josie and Janie and Effie <span class='line-break'> </span> are <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>playing cards</a> now.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 : o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-709">
<h3><a name="page-709">Tuesday, November 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a>.  I kept <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went up to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and staid with <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> children while Marvin and Carrie <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and tonight Ben and Josie <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie Gravley</a> has gone to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> at Strait <span class='line-break'> </span> Stone to a <a href='../subjects/7589' title='Community League'>Community League</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> meeting.  <a href='../subjects/7590' title='Miss Angle'>Miss Angle</a> passed <span class='line-break'> </span> here to day on her way to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7591' title='Mountain School House'>Mountain School House</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 : oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-710">
<h3><a name="page-710">Wednesday, November 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7531' title='sawing'>sawed</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> for <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a>.  Broke his <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7592' title='saw'>saw</a> and could not finish.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> done a big washing.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> heard <span class='line-break'> </span> to day that <a href='../subjects/982' title='Max Carr'>Max Carr</a> is at <a href='../subjects/7607' title='Mr Power'>Mr <span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a> to night and will leave <span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie Gravley</a> is here tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard that <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went from <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope she may be well by <span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-711">
<h3><a name="page-711">Thursday, November 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and the children went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  He hitched the <a href='../subjects/133' title='horses'>horses</a> to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/115' title='wagon'>waggon</a> and started to <span class='line-break'> </span> meet the children met them <span class='line-break'> </span> nearly at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia Harvey</a> come with <span class='line-break'> </span> Janie home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> has bin <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> all <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> .  She <span class='line-break'> </span> cooked a <a href='../subjects/17' title='chickens'>chicken</a> and made <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/169' title='coconut'>cocoanut</a> <a href='../subjects/170' title='pies'>pies</a>.  They were fine.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I have set by the <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> more than common to day <span class='line-break'> </span> and have enjoyed it.  I have <span class='line-break'> </span> had a very good fire tonight <span class='line-break'> </span> for which I am glad.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This is the night of Thanks <span class='line-break'> </span> Giving day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-712">
<h3><a name="page-712">Friday, November 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> worked on <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>house</a> until twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> then Owen and Ben and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a>.  They had <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/448' title='play'>play</a> of some sort over there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> and I staid here with <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> is here tonight Ben went <span class='line-break'> </span> to meet him.  He had to go as <span class='line-break'> </span> far as <a href='../subjects/7594' title='Jim Roland'>Jim Rolans</a>.  The[y] did <span class='line-break'> </span> not get home until after ten.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I heard today that <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I do hope that she will soon <span class='line-break'> </span> be well.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie Gravley</a> has gone home <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <a href='../subjects/7583' title='Mrs Gravley'>Mrs Gravley</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> for her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 11 30 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-713">
<h3><a name="page-713">Saturday, November 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was here.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> did not do much <span class='line-break'> </span> work.  He moved the <a href='../subjects/414' title='fence'>fence</a> so <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> could go to <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7595' title='haystacks'>straw stacks</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7596' title='baked chicken'>baked  chicken</a> and <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> <a href='../subjects/466' title='steak'>steak</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I think we all enjoyed the <span class='line-break'> </span> dinner.  <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs Carr</a> has a bad <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>colde</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben carried <span class='line-break'> </span> John to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> with them.  <a href='../subjects/7519' title='Christinia Brumfield'>Tenia</a> met John <span class='line-break'> </span> at Gretna.  He said that <span class='line-break'> </span> he would go back to <a href='../subjects/7216' title='Portsmouth, Virginia'>Portsmouth</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tomorrow.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a> carried his <span class='line-break'> </span> family to <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> to day <span class='line-break'> </span> on his <a href='../subjects/219' title='truck'>truck</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7598' title='gasoline'>Gasoline</a> gave <span class='line-break'> </span> out and he got some from Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> to get the truck home.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8: o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-714">
<h3><a name="page-714">Sunday, December  1, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> and <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> went with <a href='../subjects/936' title='Fannie Carr'>Mrs <span class='line-break'> </span> Carr</a> home.  <a href='../subjects/7601' title='Fletcher Carr'>Fletcher Carr</a> come to <span class='line-break'> </span> see his people to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> come there.  We all <span class='line-break'> </span> eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a>.  She had <span class='line-break'> </span> a nice dinner had <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/54' title='custard'>custard</a> the first that I have <span class='line-break'> </span> seen this <a href='../subjects/120' title='falling'>fall</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We are all reasonably well for <span class='line-break'> </span> which I want to feel thankful.  <span class='line-break'> </span> There is so much <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> sorrow in the country.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I never saw the like before <span class='line-break'> </span> and I am getting olde.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 : oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-715">
<h3><a name="page-715">Monday, December  2, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> had <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>corn shucking</a> had a few hands <span class='line-break'> </span> and finished his <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.  I got a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7570' title='snack'>snack</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening found them all <span class='line-break'> </span> able to be up.  Heard that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/295' title='Nellie Brumfield'>Nellie</a> and <a href='../subjects/7349' title='Evelyn Brumfield'>Evelyn Brumfield</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I am so sorry.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a box of <a href='../subjects/56' title='yarn'>yarn</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a> to day guess <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> sent it hope I will <span class='line-break'> </span> hear from her soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie and I <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some <span class='line-break'> </span> to night the first time <span class='line-break'> </span> this fall.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 o clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-716">
<h3><a name="page-716">Tuesday, December  3, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/13' title='cold'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> carried a load of <a href='../subjects/36' title='wood'>wood</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to the <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school house</a> this morning <span class='line-break'> </span> and then helped <a href='../subjects/201' title='shucking corn'>shuck corn</a> at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a>.  They got done by twelve.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening Ben and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7208' title='Altavista, Virginia'>Altavista</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie washed this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I kept <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield today and got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7602' title='Fanny'>Fanny</a> and <a href='../subjects/7603' title='Julia Emerson'>Julia Emersons</a> picture.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Tonight <a href='../subjects/424' title='Doris Brumfield'>Doris Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7386' title='Christine Reynolds'>Christine Reynolds</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> here.  They come with the <span class='line-break'> </span> children from school.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie Gravley</a> did not <span class='line-break'> </span> teach to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope I may feel better <span class='line-break'> </span> by morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-717">
<h3><a name="page-717">Wednesday, December  4, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed his hogs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> helped him.  <a href='../subjects/419' title='Travis Dews'>Mr Dews</a> <a href='../subjects/298' title='corn shucking'>shucked <span class='line-break'> </span> corn</a>.  <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> helped him.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> and staid <span class='line-break'> </span> a while.  <a href='../subjects/7604' title='Frances Callands'>Frances Callans <span class='line-break'> </span> (col'd)</a> helped Carrie to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  She <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Heard to day that <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie <span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhew</a> went to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7225' title='Steven Davis'>Steven Davis</a> and they looked <span class='line-break'> </span> for him home last night and <span class='line-break'> </span> he had not come yet tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I feel uneasy a bout him.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I do hope that nothing <span class='line-break'> </span> serious has happened to him.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He is one of our best neighbors.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-718">
<h3><a name="page-718">Thursday, December  5, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> got up <a href='../subjects/258' title='corn'>corn</a> until twelve <span class='line-break'> </span> then Ben helped <a href='../subjects/7605' title='house raising'>rais a house</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/218' title='George Hutcherson'>George Hutcherson</a>.  I went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> there.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> gave me some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim Power</a> and <a href='../subjects/7601' title='Fletcher Carr'>Fletcher <span class='line-break'> </span> Carr</a> is here to night <span class='line-break'> </span> also <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley Hutcherson</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a>.  She made Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/7606' title='shirts'>shirt</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius Gravley</a> come home from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7496' title='training camp'>camp</a> to stay we hope.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-719">
<h3><a name="page-719">Friday, December  6, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/61' title='wind'>windy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7607' title='Mr Power'>Mr Power</a> and <a href='../subjects/7608' title='Mr Carr'>Carr</a> was here <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  She fixed <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/466' title='steak'>steak</a> and made <a href='../subjects/7610' title='potato salad'>potato sallid</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  I went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>.  <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie</a> and <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johns</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>.  Two of the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/109' title='teachers'>teachers</a> went to the <span class='line-break'> </span> teachers meeting at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7611' title='Schoolfield, Virginia'>School<span class='line-break'> </span> field.</a><span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-720">
<h3><a name="page-720">Saturday, December  7, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a>.  It has bin a <span class='line-break'> </span> busy day with <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went down to the <a href='../subjects/7382' title='kitchen'>cook room</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> 15 to four oclock made a <a href='../subjects/14' title='fire'>fire</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> washed the <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> dishes then got <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a>.  Called the rest of them <span class='line-break'> </span> then we eat.  After breakfast I <span class='line-break'> </span> cut up two <a href='../subjects/7251' title='pumpkin'>pumpkins</a> and put them <span class='line-break'> </span> on to cook then put on some <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to cook <a href='../subjects/131' title='feeding'>fed</a> two <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calves</a> and brought a <span class='line-break'> </span> bucket of <a href='../subjects/123' title='water'>water</a> then <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a> two <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and sloped the <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> put on a <a href='../subjects/7612' title='liver'>liver</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/7613' title='hogs head'>face</a> to make <a href='../subjects/7278' title='scrapple'>scrappel</a> then <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/16' title='churning'>churned</a>.  Josie made <a href='../subjects/390' title='bread'>bread</a> and <a href='../subjects/114' title='coffee'>coffee</a> for <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I washed up a lot of things and took up <span class='line-break'> </span> the meat for dinner then eat dinner.  Took <span class='line-break'> </span> up the pumpkins and meat for scrapple <span class='line-break'> </span> and made the scrappel.  <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Janie Gravley</a> and <a href='../subjects/7972' title='Lucius Gravely'>Lucius</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7615' title='Muriel Gravley'>Muriel Gravley</a> and <a href='../subjects/7652' title='Effie Brumfield Cundiff'>Effie Brumfield</a> stopped <span class='line-break'> </span> here a few minutes on their way <span class='line-break'> </span> home from <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.  Well I have not <span class='line-break'> </span> room for any more.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-721">
<h3><a name="page-721">Sunday, December  8, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/68' title='John Hutcherson'>John Hutchersons</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/218' title='George Hutcherson'>George Hutcherson</a> to work on <span class='line-break'> </span> his <a href='../subjects/267' title='car'>auto</a>.  Ben come <span class='line-break'> </span> home to <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid <span class='line-break'> </span> at home all day.  <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and I went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Marvin was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>not well</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope that he may soon <span class='line-break'> </span> be well a gain.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-722">
<h3><a name="page-722">Monday, December  9, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> for the time <span class='line-break'> </span> of year.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  I went up to <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owens</a> this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning a few minutes.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I boiled the last of our <a href='../subjects/7574' title='beef'>beef</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> today.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> fried dougnuts.  <span class='line-break'> </span> We heard that <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> is <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.  I do hope that she may not <span class='line-break'> </span> be sick long.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Think now that I will go to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a> to morrow with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollie Reynolds</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and Josie and <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie Gravley</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> has all gone to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> tonight to get things for a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7616' title='fruitcake'>fruit cake</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-723">
<h3><a name="page-723">Tuesday, December 10, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day but no <span class='line-break'> </span> rain.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home and worked <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried me to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Reynolds</a> be fore light this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning.  I went with them <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/973' title='Danville, Virginia'>Danville</a>.  We was at <a href='../subjects/7617' title='Spring Garden, Virginia'>Spring <span class='line-break'> </span> Garden</a> be fore it was light <span class='line-break'> </span> good.  We saw lots of <span class='line-break'> </span> pretty things.  I did not by <span class='line-break'> </span> much.  Eat <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a> at <a href='../subjects/138' title='Mollie Reynolds'>Mollies</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and enjoyed it.  The boys <a href='../subjects/63' title='Robert Reynolds'>Robert</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floyd</a> got them a <a href='../subjects/422' title='bicycle'>bycicle</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I am at home to night<span class='line-break'> </span> O K.  <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie</a> is here <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  I enjoy having <span class='line-break'> </span> her.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-724">
<h3><a name="page-724">Wednesday, December 11, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> helped <span class='line-break'> </span> dig on <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <a href='../subjects/232' title='pit'>pit</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> carried <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie</a> and <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> this morning.  She <span class='line-break'> </span> said she liked to of froze be <span class='line-break'> </span> fore she got home.  Ben went after <span class='line-break'> </span> them this evening.  <a href='../subjects/7590' title='Miss Angle'>Miss Angle</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is spending the night here tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> and I am <span class='line-break'> </span> so troubled a bout her think <span class='line-break'> </span> I will go and see her tomorrow <span class='line-break'> </span> if I am well enough.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-725">
<h3><a name="page-725">Thursday, December 12, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> disagreeable <span class='line-break'> </span> day but no rain.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7590' title='Miss Angle'>Miss Angle</a> and <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went from here to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/29' title='sewing'>sewed</a> some.  I <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a>.  I got some <a href='../subjects/56' title='yarn'>yarn</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7212' title='Richmond, Virginia'>Richmond</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening did not stay <span class='line-break'> </span> long.  Heard to day that <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> was feeling some better.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>

<div id="page-726">
<h3><a name="page-726">Friday, December 13, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has <span class='line-break'> </span> bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Mr Owen</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> and <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William <span class='line-break'> </span> Gilbert</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed</a> two <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>hogs</a> for Ben <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  I cleaned <span class='line-break'> </span> up the <a href='../subjects/256' title='smoke house'>smoke house</a> then I took <span class='line-break'> </span> he fat off the <a href='../subjects/7618' title='entrails'>intrils</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and cleaned the feet of the hogs.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben carried <a href='../subjects/7897' title='Janie Gravely'>Miss Janie</a> home <span class='line-break'> </span> and got <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Mr Jim Emersons</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7619' title='tinsmithing'>tining tools</a>.  He wants to cover <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a> soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  <a href='../subjects/427' title='Floyd Reynolds'>Floyd Reynolds</a> come by <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening and got a few <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/249' title='eggs'>eggs</a>. He was on his <a href='../subjects/422' title='bicycle'>bycicle</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I feel like I know he broke them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-727">
<h3><a name="page-727">Saturday, December 14, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day and some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rain</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I made <a href='../subjects/7622' title='sausage'>sausage</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and dried up some <a href='../subjects/7620' title='lard'>lard</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/129' title='Denia Blair'>Denia Blair</a> and <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> come to see us this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I was glad to see them.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> has not bin well <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  I think he was <span class='line-break'> </span> very glad to see Jim.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Willie Mayhew</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/63' title='Robert Reynolds'>Robert</a> is here to night. <span class='line-break'> </span> They are <a href='../subjects/946' title='playing cards'>playing cards</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> There was a <a href='../subjects/83' title='thunder'>thunder</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> cloud to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben found <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>Lucy the cow</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> with a <a href='../subjects/87' title='calves'>calf</a> to night.</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-728">
<h3><a name="page-728">Sunday, December 15, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> bad day.  <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a> and <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> spent the day walking around.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Jim went home this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/195' title='Henry Blair'>Henry Blair</a> carried him to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> walked over to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate <span class='line-break'> </span> Harveys</a> this evening for <a href='../subjects/7297' title='Virginia Owen?'>Virginias</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> [calf? cap?].  I staid with <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Henry and <a href='../subjects/111' title='Edna Brumfield'>Edna</a> went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a while this evening.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-729">
<h3><a name="page-729">Monday, December 16, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A bad day.  <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>Rained</a> most <span class='line-break'> </span> of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I was <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a> but could <span class='line-break'> </span> not eat.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/15' title='milking'>milked</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Josie boiled <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> and made <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7278' title='scrapple'>scrappel</a> and finished drying <span class='line-break'> </span> out the <a href='../subjects/7620' title='lard'>lard</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I have <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knit</a> most of the <span class='line-break'> </span> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7621' title='Miss Snead'>Miss Snead</a> come to see <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben.  Something about the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>schools</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7561' title='Gladys Brumfield'>Gladys</a> Brumfield <span class='line-break'> </span> come with her.  I did not <span class='line-break'> </span> meet her.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> a while this <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> They were all well at Marvins.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-730">
<h3><a name="page-730">Tuesday, December 17, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a> <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed hogs</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> came down here a few <span class='line-break'> </span> minutes this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I finished <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knitting</a> for <a href='../subjects/7350' title='Thelma Brumfield'>Thelma</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Have <a href='../subjects/79' title='letter writing'>wrote</a> to <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-731">
<h3><a name="page-731">Wednesday, December 18, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kates</a> and <a href='../subjects/265' title='hog killing'>killed her <span class='line-break'> </span> hogs</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I worked on our <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7620' title='lard'>lard</a> and <a href='../subjects/7622' title='sausage'>sausage</a>.  Josie ground <span class='line-break'> </span> and made the sausage and dried <span class='line-break'> </span> up some of the lard.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I worked at the <a href='../subjects/7624' title='wash house'>wash house</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and she at the <a href='../subjects/7609' title='house'>house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben brought some things at <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1625' title='Renan, Virginia'>Renan</a> to day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a piece of <a href='../subjects/7625' title='flannel'>flanel</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> from <a href='../subjects/7209' title='Chatham, Virginia'>Chatham</a> by <a href='../subjects/7530' title='mail'>mail</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  Josie sent <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effies</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/57' title='knitting'>knitting</a> to day.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-732">
<h3><a name="page-732">Thursday, December 19, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <a href='../subjects/67' title='Willie Mayhew'>Mayhew</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> covered <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a big washin <span class='line-break'> </span> of clothes and then went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and Josie made <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I staid with the children <span class='line-break'> </span> and worked at first one <span class='line-break'> </span> thing and then another.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/7224' title='Julia Ferguson'>Julia <span class='line-break'> </span> Fergerson</a> and <a href='../subjects/7599' title='Mildred Ferguson'>her babys</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> picture.  It is fine I think.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-733">
<h3><a name="page-733">Friday, December 20, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> finished covering <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens <span class='line-break'> </span> house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> washed a gain today.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Then we all went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a>.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> and Josie made <span class='line-break'> </span> some <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> they got on fine <span class='line-break'> </span> with it.  <a href='../subjects/8130' title='Dan Shelton'>Dan Sheltons <span class='line-break'> </span> baby</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I have bin looking for a <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim Brumfield</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for several days.  I am so<span class='line-break'> </span> afraid he is <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sick</a>.   <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9:15 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-734">
<h3><a name="page-734">Saturday, December 21, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked <span class='line-break'> </span> on <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a>.  <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/240' title='cake'>cake</a> this morning and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little <span class='line-break'> </span> while then Ben and Josie went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7204' title='Straight Stone, Virginia'>Strait Stone</a> come home and <span class='line-break'> </span> made some <a href='../subjects/7396' title='pickling'>pickle</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I washed a little this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben found <a href='../subjects/134' title='hogs'>Bell</a> with five <span class='line-break'> </span> little <a href='../subjects/370' title='pigs'>pigs</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/9' title='Henry Anderson Brumfield'>Henry</a> is <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> to night.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-735">
<h3><a name="page-735">Sunday, December 22, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  We all <span class='line-break'> </span> staid at home all day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/7626' title='reading'>read</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> It has <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>cleared off</a> tonight.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> and <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> here this evening a few minutes.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-736">
<h3><a name="page-736">Monday, December 23, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day and <a href='../subjects/159' title='warm'>warm</a> for <span class='line-break'> </span> the time of the year.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a> this morning and went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/7342' title='Cedar Forest'>Cedar Forest</a> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> to day and got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> sent us some <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7628' title='oysters'>oysters</a>.  We had them for dinner <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/71' title='supper'>supper</a>.  I <a href='../subjects/7380' title='stew'>stew</a>ed <a href='../subjects/7251' title='pumpkin'>pumpkins</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> boiled <a href='../subjects/260' title='meat'>meat</a> and made <a href='../subjects/7278' title='scrapple'>scrapple</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> boiled <a href='../subjects/7345' title='beets'>beets</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Then went to <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> a little <span class='line-break'> </span> while.  Ben had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <span class='line-break'> </span> John to day heard from <a href='../subjects/141' title='Jim Brumfield'>Jim</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> He has bin <a href='../subjects/81' title='complaining'>complaining</a> with <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7629' title='rheumatism'>rheumatism</a>.  I do hope he may <span class='line-break'> </span> get well soon.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/20' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Jr.'>Franklin</a> got <a href='../subjects/7630' title='slippers'>slippers</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to day.  He was so proud of <span class='line-break'> </span> them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 10 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-737">
<h3><a name="page-737">Tuesday, December 24, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A very <a href='../subjects/49' title='rain'>rainy</a> day.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> all day.  Owen went to <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> baked some <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I <a href='../subjects/97' title='ironing'>ironed</a> most of the day.  <span class='line-break'> </span> The children tried them selves <span class='line-break'> </span> to see how tormenting they <span class='line-break'> </span> could be.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/7627' title='Reese Smith'>Reese Smith</a> come to day <span class='line-break'> </span> and brough me a box.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I have not looked in it yet.   <span class='line-break'> </span> Guess it has <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> in it.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I wish I knowed how <span class='line-break'> </span> all of the children were feeling <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  There is so much <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/10' title='sickness'>sickness</a> that I am all <span class='line-break'> </span> ways uneasy and looking <span class='line-break'> </span> for some one to get sick.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-738">
<h3><a name="page-738">Wednesday, December 25, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  The <a href='../subjects/233' title='roads'>roads</a> is very <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/186' title='mud'>muddy</a>.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> <a href='../subjects/7631' title='hunting'>hunted</a> some today. <span class='line-break'> </span>  He killed four <a href='../subjects/7312' title='rabbits'>rabbits</a> gave two of <span class='line-break'> </span> them to <a href='../subjects/75' title='William Gilbert'>William Gilbert</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I staid at home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate</a> and <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin Harvey</a> come and eat <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with us.  They drove <a href='../subjects/202' title='Prince'>Prince</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> home and Irvin brought him home.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I had a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7205' title='Effie Thornton Brumfield'>Effie Brumfield</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/216' title='Mary Brumfield'>Mary Brumfield</a> sent me a <a href='../subjects/7632' title='diary'>book <span class='line-break'> </span> to write</a> in the coming year.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Hope I may be able to write in <span class='line-break'> </span> it.  <a href='../subjects/168' title='Dick Wooding'>Dick Woodings</a> folks gave <span class='line-break'> </span> a <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a> to night.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> The children had a good time <span class='line-break'> </span> to day playing with the <span class='line-break'> </span> things they got this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got several <a href='../subjects/7633' title='presents'>presents</a> was <span class='line-break'> </span> glad of them.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Josie gathered a bunch of <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7634' title='violets'>violets</a> in the <a href='../subjects/290' title='garden'>garden</a> to day </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-739">
<h3><a name="page-739">Thursday, December 26, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> worked on <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/181' title='tenant house'>Owens house</a> this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> This evening we all went <span class='line-break'> </span> to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a>.  They had <span class='line-break'> </span> a very nice <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and boiled <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>ham</a> <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a> and <a href='../subjects/7635' title='pickles'>pickles</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7636' title='Elsie East'>Elsie East</a> and <a href='../subjects/204' title='Isla Blair'>Isla</a> and <a href='../subjects/205' title='Cordie Blair'>Cordie <span class='line-break'> </span> Blair</a> was there.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> While we were away <span class='line-break'> </span> some one left some <a href='../subjects/7633' title='presents'>presents</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> for <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and I.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a pair of <a href='../subjects/7630' title='slippers'>bed room <span class='line-break'> </span> slippers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/209' title='John Brumfield'>John</a> sent them.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> sent me a <span class='line-break'> </span> box of nice <a href='../subjects/42' title='candy'>candy</a> and <a href='../subjects/307' title='Grace Brumfield'>Grace <span class='line-break'> </span> Brumfield</a> gave me a box <span class='line-break'> </span> of candy.  I thank them <span class='line-break'> </span> both.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-740">
<h3><a name="page-740">Friday, December 27, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> morning <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> this evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and family went to <a href='../subjects/7240' title='Jim Power'>Jim <span class='line-break'> </span> Powers</a>.  <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny Power</a> come <span class='line-break'> </span> with them home.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/157' title='Johnson Reynolds'>Johnson Reynolds</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> they were going to <a href='../subjects/379' title='Jim Thompson'>Jim Thompsons</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> I went with them.  I had <span class='line-break'> </span> a pleasant day.  <a href='../subjects/378' title='Alice Thompson'>Alice</a> had <span class='line-break'> </span> a very nice <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> and <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>olde ham</a> and every thing <span class='line-break'> </span> needful.  There was crowd <span class='line-break'> </span> eat dinner all kindfolks.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and Fanny Power has <span class='line-break'> </span> gone to <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lee Brumfields</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> to night.  Guess they will <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/19' title='dance'>dance</a>.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 9 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-741">
<h3><a name="page-741">Saturday, December 28, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> day.  <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> and <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7275' title='Fannie Power'>Fanny Power</a> come home this <span class='line-break'> </span> morning at three oclock.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> We had very late <a href='../subjects/26' title='breakfast'>breakfast</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Ben and <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> <a href='../subjects/281' title='setting hens'>set</a> up <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/23' title='Charles Brumfield'>Charles</a> and <a href='../subjects/7637' title='Lillian Brumfield'>Lillian Brumfields</a> <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7638' title='tombstones'>tomb stone</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben and <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> went with <span class='line-break'> </span> Fannie home.  The children <span class='line-break'> </span> staid here .  I got <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> Smith come down <span class='line-break'> </span> here a few minutes this <span class='line-break'> </span> evening.  <span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> <a href='../subjects/246' title='Paul Bennett'>Paul Bennett</a> come a <span class='line-break'> </span> little while this morning.  <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7503' title='Jim Emerson'>Jim Emerson</a> stopped in a <span class='line-break'> </span> few minutes this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 oclock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-742">
<h3><a name="page-742">Sunday, December 29, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/21' title='clear'>clear</a> <a href='../subjects/445' title='weather'>colde</a> day we were<span class='line-break'> </span> all at home this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7675' title='Charlie Hutcherson'>Charley Hutcherson</a> came here a<span class='line-break'> </span> little while this morning.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I went to <a href='../subjects/101' title='George Blair'>George Blairs</a> and eat<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a>. They had a fine dinner<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/140' title='turkey'>turkey</a> &amp; olde <a href='../subjects/248' title='ham'>ham</a> and everything<span class='line-break'> </span> else that it takes to make a good<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/259' title='meal'>meal</a>.  They had a lot of company<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> and the children<span class='line-break'> </span> eat dinner at <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carries</a>. They had<span class='line-break'> </span> a good dinner - old ham &amp; <a href='../subjects/54' title='custard'>custard</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/37' title='cakes'>cakes</a> of several kinds<span class='line-break'> </span> Ben &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a> went to <a href='../subjects/7207' title='Gretna, Virginia'>Gretna</a><span class='line-break'> </span> to meet <a href='../subjects/7621' title='Miss Snead'>Miss Snead</a>. She is <span class='line-break'> </span> at <a href='../subjects/108' title='Lee Brumfield'>Lees</a> to night. <a href='../subjects/7639' title='Whit Short'>Whit<span class='line-break'> </span> Short</a> was <a href='../subjects/118' title='burial'>buried</a> this evening<span class='line-break'> </span> 8 o'clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-743">
<h3><a name="page-743">Monday, December 30, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A good day <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/188' title='Sam Owen'>Owen</a><span class='line-break'> </span> hauled some <a href='../subjects/11' title='tobacco stalks'>stalks</a> for the <span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/175' title='cows'>cows</a>. <a href='../subjects/1627' title='Sally Joseph Carr Brumfield'>Josie</a> staid at home <span class='line-break'> </span> all day. I went with <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> &amp; <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carie</a> to <a href='../subjects/153' title='Ren Worsham'>Ren Worshams</a><span class='line-break'> </span> We had a very pleasant day<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7231' title='Ethel Worsham'>Ethel</a> had a good <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a><span class='line-break'> </span> and I certainly did enjoy it<span class='line-break'> </span> I am glad that Ren has a<span class='line-break'> </span> nice good house.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> Ben &amp; Josie has gone to <a href='../subjects/183' title='Mr Mayhew'>Mr<span class='line-break'> </span> Mayhews</a> to a <a href='../subjects/48' title='party'>party</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/7497' title='Reuben Reynolds'>Reubin Reynolds</a><span class='line-break'> </span> came by on their way<span class='line-break'> </span> to Mayhews. <a href='../subjects/308' title='Hugh Brumfield'>Hugh Brumfield</a><span class='line-break'> </span> is here to nigh it seems<span class='line-break'> </span> that they can't go to sleep.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> I got a <a href='../subjects/88' title='letter'>letter</a> from<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/64' title='Lottie Craddock'>Lottie Craddock</a> I am always<span class='line-break'> </span> glad to hear from them<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 10 o'clock</p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
<div id="page-744">
<h3><a name="page-744">Tuesday, December 31, 1918</a></h3>
<div class="page-content">
<p>A <a href='../subjects/1' title='cloud'>cloudy</a> day. <a href='../subjects/4' title='Benjamin Franklin Brumfield, Sr.'>Ben</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7641' title='feed cutting'>cut</a> <a href='../subjects/174' title='feed'>feed</a> at <a href='../subjects/5' title='Marvin Smith'>Marvins</a> &amp; at home.<span class='line-break'> </span> Marvin eat <a href='../subjects/28' title='dinner'>dinner</a> with Ben.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went to Marvins and spent<span class='line-break'> </span> the day. <a href='../subjects/53' title='Kate Harvey'>Kate Harvey</a> was there<span class='line-break'> </span> two.  <a href='../subjects/32' title='Carrie Smith'>Carrie</a> had a nice dinner.<span class='line-break'> </span> I went with Kate home to spend<span class='line-break'> </span> the night. <a href='../subjects/1630' title='Virginia Harvey'>Virginia</a> &amp; <a href='../subjects/52' title='Irvin Harvey'>Irvin</a><span class='line-break'> </span> went to <a href='../subjects/254' title='school'>school</a>. Irvin got a<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/148' title='helmet'>helmet</a> that they called a <a href='../subjects/7642' title='German helmet'>German<span class='line-break'> </span> helmet</a>. <a href='../subjects/59' title='Charles Harvey'>Charles Harvey</a> sent it to<span class='line-break'> </span> him.  <span class='line-break'> </span> Heard to day that<span class='line-break'> </span> <a href='../subjects/7643' title='Mrs. Pleas Worsham'>Mrs. Pleas Worsham</a> is <a href='../subjects/96' title='death'>dead</a>. <span class='line-break'> </span> It is with a sad heart<span class='line-break'> </span> that I write for the last<span class='line-break'> </span> time in my little book.<span class='line-break'> </span></p>
<p> 8 o clock </p>
</div>
</div>
<br />
